General Committee Discusses Exchange of Warship Information; Japan Opposes British, French, and Italian Proposals 43

London. The Naval Conference's General Committee met in the afternoon to discuss the proposals made by the United Kingdom, France, and Italy regarding the exchange of information on warship construction programs. Japan has expressed opposition to these proposals, making the prospect of a compromise even more remote. At today's meeting, the British representative first delivered a speech, saying that the objections previously raised by Japan to the proposals made by the United Kingdom can also be applied to the proposals of France and Italy. Therefore, these objections have already been known to all countries and do not need to be raised again. The Japanese representative replied that the new proposals of France and Italy are not in line with Japan's claim to achieve naval equality through a common maximum limit, and do not provide for a genuine method of reducing naval armaments. Among them, it is advocated to implement quantitative limitations according to the budgetary capabilities of each country. This method is still feasible. However, this still fails to satisfy Japan's claim to obtain security through naval equality. The British representative then explained that once the exchange of warship construction program information is implemented, any country wishing to launch the construction of new ships can know about it in advance and take preventive measures, or immediately conduct negotiations in the hope of reaching an agreement to avoid naval competition. This method is very good. The French representative then explained the proposals made by his country, saying that this is the minimum condition for naval powers to reach an agreement. France advocates that its warship construction program be notified six months in advance. This method is sufficient to keep the path of negotiation open, and countries can notify each other of warship construction programs within a year without taking measures with a one-year deadline. The Italian representative supported the French view, and the American representative also said that this proposal is worthy of full consideration. (Havas Dispatch, 8th)

London. The First Committee met at 3:18 p.m. on the 8th. Nagano and Nagai, both plenipotentiaries, and Specialist Committee member Iwashita attended. Chairman Monsell announced the opening of the meeting and presented the British government's declaration on warship construction, arguing that under the current circumstances, there is no way to avoid warship construction competition except by adopting this plan. The representatives of France and Italy also presented their respective notification plans and explained the contents. The representatives of the various countries began to discuss, but the content has not yet left the initial scope. However, Plenipotentiary Nagano, in accordance with the established policy, declared the Japanese government's attitude towards the warship notification plan, saying that from the essence of military reduction, the warship notification plan is only a matter belonging to the second issue. The London and Washington Treaties use this plan as a success for quantitative restriction of military reduction, and the most important thing is to strive for the achievement of quantitative restriction first. If there is no special topic for deliberation in the quantitative restriction plan, please deliberate on the Japanese government's common maximum limit issue. After Plenipotentiary Nagano finished speaking, the representatives of the United Kingdom, the United States, France, Italy, and the Dominions unanimously formed a common front to deal with Plenipotentiary Nagano, arguing that the warship notification plan is the main issue of the quantitative restriction plan. Why is Japan avoiding the notification plan, and demanding that Nagano participate in the discussion of this plan? However, Nagano insisted on his own view from beginning to end and did not give in. Chairman Monsell, due to the chaotic arguments, announced that Japan was unwilling to participate in the discussion of the warship notification plan and announced the adjournment of the meeting at 4:46 p.m., deciding to hold the next meeting at 3:00 p.m. on the 10th. (Domei Dispatch, 8th)

Mediterranean and Atlantic - British and French Naval Rotation - First Sound of Collective Action 44

London - The British naval support fleet will withdraw from the Mediterranean, while 91 French warships stationed in the Atlantic will sail to the Mediterranean. Well-informed observers here regard this as the first result of the collective security policy. The rumor of the French authorities sending ships to the Mediterranean has been circulating for a long time. However, the news that four warships of the British Home Fleet sailed back to their country from Gibraltar was quite sudden. Officials are still keeping the Home Fleet's actions a secret. However, Berlin reports that this is part of a grand defense plan of France and Britain, aimed at dealing with Germany and Italy. The authorities have firmly denied this. It is generally believed that the current actions of the French and British fleets are the result of the British government's insistence that if Mussolini takes "mad dog actions," France and Britain should jointly deal with it. At the same time, it is believed that Franco-Italian relations are not very friendly. In Mussolini's eyes, the appearance of French warships in the Mediterranean is not as hateful as that of British warships. (Reuters, 8th)

London - The French naval fleet has recently been moving along the Atlantic and North African coasts of the Mediterranean. It is believed here that although no agreement has been concluded regarding naval cooperation between Britain and France, the actions of the French navy are to meet the needs of Anglo-French cooperation. According to naval sources, the French naval fleet will likely be stationed near the Strait of Gibraltar so that it can contact the French Mediterranean Fleet when the British Navy needs French assistance. These sources also believe that although the British warships "Hotspur," "Renown," and cruisers "Orion," "Neptune," etc., originally stationed in the Mediterranean area will be withdrawn to their country (as reported earlier), the strategic importance of the British fleet currently stationed in the Strait of Gibraltar will not change as a result. These warships have been stationed abroad for a long time and need to be repaired. To maintain the morale of the navy, their soldiers also need to rest. This is why the Navy Department is recalling these warships to their country. (Havas, 8th)

London - A Navy Department spokesperson stated that the rumor that the British Main Fleet intended to cruise the Mediterranean area was a mistake, referring to the Atlantic. However, the spokesperson did not specify where the fleet would cruise in the Atlantic. Today, newspapers published news of the French naval movement with alarming headlines. Official sources said that this move by the French navy was not at the behest of Britain and was absolutely unrelated to the talks held by the Anglo-French staff in Paris. As for the warships "Hotspur," cruiser "Remillies," "Orion," "Neptune," etc., being recalled to their country, this is also unrelated to the cruise of the French fleet. After these warships return to their country, their defensive duties will be taken over by the warships "Nelson," "Rodney," cruiser "Cairo," and aircraft carrier "Furious." (Havas, 8th)

Paris - According to the announcement issued by the Navy Department on December 21st of last year, the Second Naval Fleet will soon sail to the West African Atlantic coast for exercises, which will last for several weeks. Because the winter climate in the Brittany waters is severely cold and not suitable for exercises, the exercises were changed to the coast of West Africa. The commander of the Second Fleet is Vice Admiral Darlan. The ships under his command will depart from their base on the 14th of this month and arrive at the port of Casablanca on the Moroccan coast of Africa on the 18th. From there, they will sail to the ports of Abidjan and Dakar in French West Africa and be stationed there until the 26th of this month, and meet with the cruisers "Emile Bertin" and "Courageous," currently stationed in the West Indies. (Havas, 9th)

London - In early December of last year, Britain asked Spain whether, if the British Navy in the Mediterranean were attacked by Italy after implementing an oil embargo, Spain was prepared to immediately assist Britain. The Spanish government has not yet replied to this question. (According to sources, the governments of Turkey, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Greece have already accepted the naval mutual assistance plan.) It is generally known that Spain will submit a reply after the general election in March. Regarding the oil embargo issue, the British government may propose it at the League of Nations Council meeting on the 20th of this month. Member states of the League of Nations should automatically implement a mutual assistance system for any new embargo measures and formulate detailed rules for this mutual assistance system as a condition for intensifying sanctions against Italy. However, it is generally felt that Britain does not intend to propose expanding the scope of sanctions on its own. If other countries have such a suggestion, France will support it, but only on the condition that the entire mutual assistance plan is stipulated. Regarding this, some quarters believe that, after Italian planes bombed the Swedish ambulance team on the southern route of Abyssinia, Sweden may be the first to demand the implementation of an oil embargo. (Havas, 8th)

Paris - According to a correspondent for the Daily Mail in Berlin, after several newspapers in London published news of military cooperation between Britain and France, German political figures paid close attention to this issue, believing that cooperation between Britain and France was by no means temporary and would continue to exist even after a final resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute was reached. "German figures firmly believe that the agreement negotiated by the staff of Britain and France must be effective for a long period of time. The fact that Britain did not sign an agreement with Germany, but directly established a mutual assistance plan with France, has violated the obligations that the signatories of the Locarno Treaty should fulfill." The correspondent also said that the German government will soon ask the British and French governments how this mutual assistance plan can be integrated with the obligations stipulated in the Locarno Treaty. (Havas, 9th)

Russian-Japanese War Inevitable - Observations of Sir Arthur Hyde - Red Army Assembling in the Far East, Situation Tense - Border Disputes, Russia Accused of Reporting False Facts 53

London - The Royal Civil Servants Association recently held a meeting here to discuss the prospects for future wars in the Far East. The Nagoya Shimbun reported that since the breakdown of the Manchu-Mongolian Conference and the establishment of the Anti-Communist Committee in North China, Outer Mongolia's policy towards Manchuria has become more active, resulting in frequent conflicts on the Manchu-Mongolian border. Moscow - Japanese newspapers carried Changchun dispatches stating that the Kwantung Army announced that "On December 28th of last year, six Soviet bandits intruded into Manchurian territory near a small mountain north of Yangshengzi on the eastern border of "Manchukuo" and abducted 26 Manchurians and six horses back into Soviet territory." The announcement also stated that "The place where the Manchurians were abducted is clearly Manchurian territory."

TASS is now instructed to declare that the above announcement by the Kwantung Army completely distorts the truth. According to a subsequent investigation, the truth is as follows: on December 28th of last year, 28 Manchurian loggers were ordered by contractors to cut timber for the Japanese military police near the Pan Huan River. They intruded into Soviet territory between the 23rd and 24th border defense battalions southwest of Tu Heluo Ge and cut Soviet timber in the Shiremetiev Valley. They stepped into Soviet territory 1.5 kilometers. They cut a large amount of timber and were immediately detained by the Soviet border guards and handed over to the border commander. TASS has also learned that a team of 15 Japanese and "Manchu" soldiers appeared at the logging site on January 4th. They penetrated 300 meters into Soviet territory. They saw the Soviet border patrol from afar and immediately retreated into Manchurian territory. The Kwantung Army Headquarters must know the reason for the loggers' detention. Therefore, its announcement is undoubtedly a deliberate fabrication. (TASS, 9th)

US Senate Committee - Investigation of Arms Developments - Evidence Obtained of Supplying Arms During European War 57

Washington - The Senate Committee investigating the supply of arms and finance during the European War met this morning and obtained evidence showing that a company related to the famous international banker J.P. Morgan sold ammunition, war materials, food, clothing, medical supplies, etc., worth 363,000,000 yuan to Britain and France before the United States joined the Great War. It also showed that Morgan warned Britain not to cancel the order for 45,000,000 yuan worth of rifles. Morgan purchased rifles worth a total of 194,000,000 yuan for the British and Russian armies in 1915. The Senate Committee has a telegram issued by Morgan, which instructed its branch in London to report to the British authorities on the content of the US government's third note to Germany regarding the sinking of the Lusitania by a German submarine. The telegram was sent six weeks before the US third note was issued, stating, "It has been learned from confidential sources that the US President's reply to Germany earnestly requires Germany to first address the moral issues of this matter. US cabinet members attach great importance to this matter. This matter should be resolved by Germany. The United States has no other choice." (Reuters, 8th)

Austrian Premier and Foreign Minister to Visit Hungary and Czechoslovakia 58

Berlin: Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg will visit Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, in the coming days. Foreign Minister Guido Schmidt will also visit Budapest, the capital of Hungary. Diplomatic sources here speculate that Austrian foreign policy has shifted due to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. The Austrian government believes that Italy's strength has been weakened by its war against Abyssinia, and the value of Austria's friendship with Italy has diminished. Therefore, Austria intends to seek support from the Little Entente countries to maintain the "Anschluss" (union with Austria) objective. As for Foreign Minister Schmidt's visit to Hungary, it is mainly to reassure Hungary, which may feel uneasy after Austria's closer ties with the Little Entente. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

U.S. Army Victory Over British Anniversary: Roosevelt Criticizes Anti-Government Faction; Voters Should Be Above Representatives of the Bourgeoisie; Ordinary Citizens Should Enjoy a Better Life 59

Washington: Today marks the anniversary of the American independent army's great victory over the British army in New Orleans in 1815. President Roosevelt addressed the nation, first mentioning President Jackson's support for democratic republicanism and his deadly battle against the domestic material power opposition. He then stated that in the past thirty-four months, history has repeated itself, which urgently needs to be clarified. Difficult problems have reappeared today, and the facts are more complex than before because the opposition is trying hard to distort and conceal the truth. Regardless of his political program in the future presidential election or who the Democratic presidential candidate is, the preservation of democratic government is the fundamental issue. He recently received letters from thousands of strangers expressing agreement with his statement that only a minority in the business and financial sectors want to resist the freedom of the people. He is very grateful for these letters. As for the Supreme Court's ruling that the Agricultural Adjustment Act (AAA) is invalid, he cannot criticize it, but its final result will affect the lives of Americans for many years. In short, seeking justice and prosperity for American agriculture remains the most urgent and unwavering goal of the current government. Since we bear the responsibility of leadership, fulfilling the expectations of young men and women across America is our solemn responsibility. President Roosevelt also said that the United States is not competing with the world, but the battles fought within our borders today are economic, not territorial, and our enemies are the forces of privilege and greed within the country. The American people should know the purpose of their government, and we will never retreat. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Washington: Since the Supreme Court rejected the Agricultural Adjustment Act (AAA), President Roosevelt has not made any comments. However, today, at the Democratic Party's memorial dinner for President Jackson, he used radio broadcasting to launch a severe criticism of the forces attacking the government's policies. Roosevelt recounted the hardships and difficulties Jackson encountered during the fierce battle with the British army in New Orleans in 1812, and then claimed that the government's current situation is the same as Jackson's. After expressing his respect for the Democratic Party, which elected Jackson as president, Roosevelt called on the people of the country to unite and support the current government's policies in order to fight against the opposition. Although Roosevelt did not explicitly name the opposition forces or mention the Supreme Court's decision, the meaning of his speech was very clear, that is, the court's decision cannot overturn the laws passed by the elected Congress. The President stated that Jackson's struggle for democracy and politics was aimed at achieving justice and fairness. Only in this way, capitalists and newspapers at the time unanimously opposed his policies. President Jackson firmly believed that the decision of the voters should be higher than the decision of the minority representing the power of large assets, and ordinary citizens should have the right to enjoy a better life. However, those who opposed Jackson were the ruthless and cruel people of the time and the traditional forces that were behind the times. In this environment, Jackson sometimes felt that the power of the opposition was all over the country, but in reality, the people of the country were standing on the same front as Jackson. Today's situation can be said to be the same as in Jackson's era. We must maintain the democratic government as the fundamental issue of the future general election. I firmly believe that the American people will recognize the government's purpose and support our policies. We have no need to retreat. (National Telegram, 8th)

U.S. House Committee Considers Relieving Farmers' Suffering; Drafting a Plan to Replace the AAA 60

Washington: The House Agriculture Committee today began drafting a new law to replace the Agricultural Adjustment Act (AAA), which was ruled invalid by the Supreme Court on Monday. The committee chairman, Democratic Congressman Jones, claimed that they would be able to devise another plan within the scope of the Supreme Court's judgment to alleviate the suffering of farmers under the current tax laws. The plans currently under consideration by the committee include the following five points: 1. Plans for domestic agricultural products; 2. Subsidy plans for agricultural product exports; 3. Providing financial assistance to states that independently implement adjustment plans similar to the AAA; 4. Allocating funds to rent farmland and temporarily suspend cultivation to restore soil fertility; 5. Providing conditional assistance to individuals who can prove that they are following the production restriction plan. (National Telegram, 8th)

New York: Two Indiana bread factories today petitioned the court to recover the $1,800 in procedural donations collected by the government under the now-invalidated AAA. It is expected that hundreds of lawsuits seeking to recover the procedural donations that have already been paid will follow. This is just the beginning. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

The Financial Crisis of Militarist Japan (Part 1) 61

— Huang Fu

As usual, the Japanese political season begins in early November after the Army University maneuvers. This year (1935), due to the "clarification of the corporate personality of the state" (團體明徵) issue, there was indeed a stir in the usually "idle" months of August and September. The "weak" Okada cabinet barely issued two statements thoroughly refuting the "organ theory of the state" (機關說), and organized a "Council on Education Reform" (敎學評議會) for the purpose of "renovating education" (文敎刷新), temporarily easing the atmosphere of the "October Coup" (十月政變). After October, the central political circles are usually calm and uneventful during the Army University maneuvers, but this year, the Seiyukai (政友會) caused some turmoil due to their dissatisfaction with the Council on Education Reform. In late November and late December, the formal political season arrived. The former's focus was on compiling the budget for the coming year, and the latter's focus was on dealing with the Diet (國會). Therefore, the "Okada-maru" (岡田丸), manipulated by "Hermit Wani-mizu" (鰐水居士), was always tossing and turning in the stormy political sea, and its future was still shrouded in many worrying atmospheres.

In the past, when the so-called "political parties" were in power, the preliminary skirmishes in the political struggle centered on budget issues were far less serious than the debate battles that began in late December. But times have changed. Since the September 18th Incident (九一八事變), Japan has been experiencing a long and almost endless era of emergency. The struggle against political parties has become secondary or tertiary. The most tense, harmonious, and appealing program in the political season has become the military budget, starring the Ministry of Finance (大藏省) and the military (軍部). Will the 82-year-old "half-immortal, half-mortal" (半仙半俗) Finance Minister Takahashi win, or will the vigorous military win? This is the focus of attention for all of Japan, and perhaps the world.

Since the September 18th Incident, Japan's military spending has increased sharply every year. In addition to the regular military expenditures such as the army and navy's pay, subsidies for heavy industry, etc., direct military expenditures have already accounted for more than 46% of the total national budget. In order to fill this huge "extraordinary expenditure," Japan has issued "deficit bonds" (赤字公債) that have almost reached the limit. Most of these flood-like bonds are stored in the vaults of the banking industry. It is clear that the most worrying issue for Japanese financial capitalists at present is how to curb the issuance of deficit bonds so that it does not exceed the scope that would cause "malignant inflation" (惡性Inflation). Therefore, the first valuable promise that Takahashi, who is respected by bankers as a "sage" (仙人), made to financiers was the "gradual reduction of deficit bonds" (赤字公債)漸减主義). However, on the other hand, the military believes that the crisis of 1936 is imminent, the Naval Disarmament Preparatory Conference held in London this year has no hope of success, the Pacific will be in a state of armament without treaties in the future, and the Soviet Union's second five-year plan has achieved more success than expected. Moreover, it is necessary to urgently implement the continental policy towards China. Therefore, in the next year's budget, they put forward a huge demand of 600 million yen for the army and 730 million yen for the navy (including 340 million yen for the army's new requirements and 300 million yen for the navy's new requirements). According to the original budget plan submitted by the Ministry of Finance to the cabinet meeting on November 26, in 1936 (Showa 11), the ordinary section of annual revenue will be 1,448,000 (thousand yen), and the temporary section will be 789,000 (including 122,000 in ordinary revenue and 666,800 in bond money), totaling 2,238,000 thousand yen. That is, even if 666.8 million yen in deficit bonds are issued next year, the annual revenue will only be 2.238 billion yen. Now, it is really a bit difficult for a clever woman - no, a "sage" - to cook without rice (巧婦——不「仙人」難為無米之炊) to spend the 1.33 billion yen of military expenses requested by the military from these 2.2 billion yen!

Let's take a look at this year's budget. "In the Showa 10 budget, with an estimated 2.2 billion yen, military spending accounts for more than 1 billion yen. Ordinary revenue is not enough to cover expenditures, so 750 million yen in deficit bonds were issued. This is just like a salaried worker (薪水生活者) who earns 65 yen a month trying to live a life of 100 yen a month. The 35 yen that is not enough is debt. Presumably because the times are bad, 47 yen out of this 100 yen is used as 'self-protection fee' (護身費)!" (Showa 11 Asahi Yearbook, page 146).

The "self-protection fee" mentioned here has already exceeded the necessity of "self-protection" in substance and is heavily tinged with adventurous nature. It is not enough to protect oneself, but also to draw the defense line to the neighbor's "inner core area" (內房重地), and even to use the name of self-protection to attack others. Then it is of course within expectation that this salaried worker who receives 65 yen a month is not enough to cover the expenses.

The amount of this "self-protection fee" and the source of borrowing have become important goals of the annual budget struggle since the beginning of the extraordinary times. The political keynote of the Okada cabinet, in addition to the strong naval color, is mainly supported by the "group of senior statesmen" (重臣集團) who have close ties with financial capital and the Minseito (民政黨), which can be regarded as the direct agent of the banking industry. Therefore, from the perspective of the interests of the banking industry, the only "sound" (健全的) means is to stop the bond policy (at least a gradual reduction in bonds) and change to "general" (一般的) tax increases. However, general tax increases are not only opposed by the military industry, but the "extremely exhausted" (疲敝已極) rural areas at present also face the danger of being unable to withstand further levies. At the time of the 1934-5 budget, when Finance Minister Fujii issued a huge amount of bonds but was still not enough to meet the military's demands, he proposed a partial tax increase plan. This tax increase aroused great resentment in the military industry and the textile industry. Later, due to the decline in the price of securities, Finance Minister Fujii resigned due to "illness," and the banking industry again invited the "half-immortal, half-mortal" Takahashi to come out of the mountain to serve as a "barrier" (壁障) for the banking industry's pressure on the military. Takahashi Korekiyo (高橋是淸), this 80-year-old man, is not only the elder of the Seiyukai, a senior statesman of the country, and a senior member of the banking industry, but his political weight and prestige have already transcended party affiliation and are considered a "national treasure" (國寳). The banking industry and the business community knew that only he could "speak" (講話) to the military, so after Fujii's failure, they finally disregarded everything and invited this mentally vigorous old man out again.

At the beginning of the budget struggle, as usual, each province sets its price, and the Minister of Finance makes a "ruling" (裁定). This year's budget, as mentioned above, the military's asking price is more than 1.33 billion yen, which is clearly a large gap from the Ministry of Finance's original plan. All other budgets have long been ignored by people. Everyone's eyes are focused on the wonderful final act of the old Finance Minister versus the military. In Japan in recent years, there is a popular saying called "Eat him or be eaten by him?" (吃他呢還是被他吃？) This tense scene is very similar to this idiom. After a long period of silent observation, the evening newspaper on November 28 published the statement of Finance Minister Takahashi on the budget policy in large letters. The original text of the statement is:

"From the point of view of the lack of natural resources, it can also be known that whether Japan can be self-sufficient in isolation is still a question. Looking at the world situation, the first country to encounter difficulties in the future is Italy, but Italy still has the support of France. Because of its relationship with Germany, France must unite with Italy. But what about Japan? Japan is encountering the jealousy of various countries due to the significant progress of industry and trade. We should carefully think about our own country! Therefore, the budget should also be compiled according to the income of the people. Financial credit is intangible, and maintaining this credit is the most urgent task. If we only pay attention to national defense, it will eventually cause malignant inflation and destroy credit, and national defense will never be consolidated! In case of an emergency, we should have some preparation and leeway, but looking back at the domestic situation, it is a time of constant natural disasters and withering people's livelihood. There are many places in social policy that are worth considering, and the military is also asked to consider this carefully!..."

The original text is quoted at length, not only to explain the crux of this budget, but mainly because this statement most clearly expresses the attitude of Japanese financiers towards the current international situation. The above Takahashi statement seems to be a matter of course on the face of it, but in modern Japan, only Takahashi Korekiyo can publicly represent bankers to say such things! The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun commented on this statement: "He dared to say what should be said but cannot be said in the symposium, and what the people should hope for but cannot hope for! The old Finance Minister is still healthy!" It is really not without basis.

Page 9

International Commercial Telegraph: Special Commercial Report from Reuters on January 9th 86

Gold and Silver

British Gold: Today's London gold price was 140 shillings, 11.5 pence, a decrease of one penny.

British Silver: Today in the London silver market, the spot price was not yet settled.

American Silver: Today in the Monterrey silver market, the opening bid was slightly lower than yesterday, while the asking price was higher than yesterday.

Exchange Rates

Today in the London foreign exchange market, the US dollar price was weak. The opening US-UK exchange rate was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 3 fen, 8125, higher than yesterday's US-UK closing rate by 1875. It fell by 125 in the first hour. In the following two hours, merchants were even more uneasy, fearing that the United States would experience inflation. The reasons are: 1. There was a large sale of silver in the market; 2. The US budget is impossible to balance; 3. The US government is about to request Congress to raise funds to repay existing agricultural debts. At 12:30 pm, the British exchange rate was 6875 higher than at 11 am. In the next half hour, it continued to rise by half a fen to 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen, 875. At 1:30 pm, it rose another half a fen to 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 5 fen, 375. However, a reaction occurred at this time, so the exchange rate fell by half a fen within 15 minutes. As a result, the exchange rate at 1:43 pm was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen, 875.

Errors in Higher Examination Questions: Examination Yuan Voluntarily Requests Punishment, Central Political Council Resolves to Punish Niu Yongjian with a Month's Salary 87

Nanjing Dispatch: Due to errors in the questions of this year's higher examination, Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan, considering his responsibility, specifically submitted a report to the Central Political Council requesting punishment. The Central Political Council resolved on the 8th that, regarding the error in the questions of this year's higher examination, Niu Yongjian, Chairman of the Examination Committee, would be punished with a month's salary. The request for punishment from the President of the Examination Yuan and Chairman of the Examination Committee should not be discussed. At the same time, Xu Mo, a member of the Examination Committee, also felt deeply disturbed that his error in drafting the questions made it difficult to escape the blame for negligence, causing Chairman Niu to take the blame for him. He has already sent apologies to President Dai and Chairman Niu, and made appropriate expressions. The original report from the Examination Yuan is recorded below: Respectfully presented is the report from Niu Yongjian, Chairman of the First Examination Committee for the Higher Examination, dated December 13, 24th year, stating that on November 26th of this year, he received a report from Chen Daqi, Director of the First Examination Office of the Higher Examination, stating, "This morning, during the second test of the higher examination for general administrative personnel, when examining the elective subject of international law, after distributing the question papers, some examinees claimed that the first question on the paper had the words 'territorial' (地域), which was actually a mistake for the words 'easement' (地役), and asked how to answer and whether to correct it. It was immediately informed that this question paper was printed and issued by the Examination Committee. The office had no right to intervene in whether the word 'territorial' was wrong. If the examinees believed that the word 'territorial' in the question was indeed a mistake for the word 'easement', they could answer according to the meaning of the word 'easement'. After this explanation, all examinees were satisfied, and the order was as usual, etc." Upon hearing this situation, Yongjian was extremely alarmed. After investigation, it was found that there were three categories for the elective subject of international law for this type of examination. After discussing with the relevant committee, it was decided that the test papers for this subject would be graded on two questions for the first question, whether it was made incorrectly or not, so as to provide relief. Although the rights of the examinees are not impaired, Yongjian's negligence cannot be excused. The matter has been reported truthfully, respectfully requesting the examination and verification of the report and forwarding it to the National Government for strict punishment, so as to emphasize the examination administration. Not daring to wait in fear for orders, and also according to the report from Chen Daqi, Chairman of the Examination Committee, dated December 15, 24th year, the First Examination Committee for the Higher Examination, when examining the elective subject of international law in the second test for general administrative personnel, mistakenly wrote the word '役' (yi, service) in the term '地役權' (di yi quan, easement) as '域' (yu, territory). Now, the facts of how this error occurred are reported to you one by one. It is said that this higher examination was decided by this committee to hold nine categories, and the category of construction personnel already included ten sub-categories. Later, it was approved by the Ministry of Communications to simultaneously hold special examinations, postal personnel examinations, and senior postal worker examinations, in reality, there were nineteen categories. Each category of examination, in the first higher examination, Chuanxian was ordered to preside over the examination, and the incident of discovering a miscalculation of the score of examinee Liu Xizhang was immediately reported to the National Government and was punished with a fine of three months' salary, and Secretary-General Chen Daqi was fined one month's salary. The discipline was strict, and it was nothing more than maintaining the fairness of the examination, according to the government's clarity. This decision that the word '役' (yi, service) in the international law question of the higher examination was mistakenly written as '城' (cheng, city), although it was a homophonic error, is still difficult to escape negligence. The cause of this incident, tracing back to the end, is that, as claimed by the Examination Committee's report, there are many subjects, the time limit is tight, and there is not enough time for detailed proofreading for question preparation and writing. Moreover, the questions involve various disciplines, and it is difficult for the chairman of the examination committee to know everything. Although he should be responsible for the oversight, it is not without excusable reasons. Chuanxian, who is in charge of the examination administration, really cannot avoid his responsibility. In addition to reporting to the National Government, he should also report to your council to strictly punish Chuanxian and the Chairman of the Examination Committee, Chen Daqi, and the Chairman of the Examination Committee, Niu Yongjian, in order to emphasize the examination administration and show impartiality. Not daring to wait in fear for orders, respectfully presented to the Central Political Council, President of the Examination Yuan, Dai Chuanxian, (January 8th)

Xiamen Taiwanese Purchase Land: Overseas Chinese Raise Funds to Redeem 88

—Taiwanese Agree to Redeem at Original Price—

Xiamen Communication: The land of Maohou Village in Heshan, outside Xiamen City, was sold by Zhou Xingnan, a former official of the Municipal Office, to the Xiamen Ken Zhi Company, organized by Taiwanese Japanese national Lin Tumu, for reclamation, covering tens of thousands of acres. The land is adjacent to the Huli Mountain Fort, a fortress in Xiamen, which is a national defense zone and has long been designated as a national defense forest. The sale to Xiamen Ken Zhi Company has aroused strong opposition from the Xiamen people. Two years ago, the Committee of All Circles Opposing Zhou Xingnan's Theft of National Land was organized, and along with the Taikoo Warehouse case, they repeatedly filed complaints to the Central Government. Last autumn, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Lin Shaonan, a diplomatic inspector of Fujian and Zhejiang, to Xiamen to handle the matter. Except for the Taikoo case, which was handled separately, at that time, Lin Tumu stated that the land reclaimed by the Xiamen Ken Zhi Company could be redeemed by the Chinese side at the original purchase price and the funds used for reclamation equipment. The people of Heshan then sent Chen Junong to Nanyang, Singapore, to raise funds from overseas Chinese from Heshan to redeem the land. After Chen arrived, the Heshan Association in Singapore held a meeting and decided to organize the "Heshan Nanhua Kenmu Company" with a fixed capital of 50,000 yuan, using 37,000 yuan for land redemption and the remainder as working capital to continue reclamation. Twenty-one preparation members were elected to jointly raise shares with Chen Junong. The capital subscribed by the Heshan Association in Singapore has reached 20,000 national currency. At the same time, the Fujian Association in Singapore also sent Zhou Xianrui, Hou Xiyou, and Tang Xiangfan to assist in raising shares. When the full amount is raised, the Heshan Association in Singapore and the Fujian Association have decided to each send a representative to accompany Chen back to China to handle the recovery of the Maohou land and all related matters. (January 8th)

Border Region Headquarters Executes Large Number of Bandit Leaders

Hankou Communication: The remote counties in western Hubei were previously harassed by the bandits He Long and Xiao Ke. Xu Yuanquan telegraphed the Pacification Headquarters on the 8th, reporting that the important captured bandits who have been approved for execution total 15: (1) Peng Zhengnan, former political commissar of the pseudo-Longsang County, later commander of the pseudo-Independent Third Regiment; (2) Pu Wanlin, chairman of the pseudo-Tongche Township government, extorting and levying taxes, causing great harm to the local area; (3) Zhou Yawei, commander of the pseudo-18th Division, 52nd Regiment, repeatedly resisting us stubbornly; (4) Zhou Haichen, political commissar of the 2nd Battalion of the pseudo-52nd Regiment; (5) Wang Xueqin, political commissar of the 3rd Battalion of the 52nd Regiment; (6) Peng Changzhi, political commissar of the pseudo-Ciyantang Township; (7) Qian Shantong, bandit leader of the Western Hubei Allied English Association, He Long's teacher, who spared no effort to support redization and anesthetize the psychology of the bandits; (8) Zhou Yunlong, bandit leader of the Western Hubei Divine Soldiers, former chief of staff of the pseudo-18th Division, who led Xiao He to harm the national army this summer. After the defeat of the bandit troops, he still gathered the defeated bandits, hoping to revive; (9) Mi Dequan, military minister of the pseudo-Xinglong District, expanded the Red Army, coercing and inducing, and once led the crowd to plunder people's homes; (10) Pan Eryin, political commissar of the pseudo-Ciyantang District, expanded propaganda with extraordinary effort; (11) Liu Guangbing, section chief of the pseudo-Longsang County government, who specialized in collecting grain, causing much harm; (12) Lin Yunqing, detective of the pseudo-52nd Regiment, adventurous and extremely fierce; (13) Liu Mingyue, squad leader of the pseudo-Young Pioneers, who raped women and instigated the killing of her husband; (14) Tian Xuejun, chairman of the pseudo-Xiang Su Fan (Township Anti-Revolution); (15) Tian Bingcheng, soldiers of the pseudo-4th Division, 10th Regiment, and the pseudo-18th Division, 52nd Regiment, deeply banditized, and suspected of spying. Except for Peng Changzhi, Tian Xuejun, and Tian Bingcheng, who were approved to reduce their sentences to fixed-term imprisonment, the rest were approved for execution. Respectfully reported. (8th)

Fuzhou: Financial Relief Measures 90

Establishment of Relief Committee: Approval for Real Estate Mortgages

Fuzhou Communication: The Fujian Provincial Government, in view of the recent financial stagnation in the provincial capital, and upon repeated requests for relief from the Minhou County Chamber of Commerce, approved a joint loan of one million yuan from the Central, China, and Communications Banks for relief. It also separately appointed the Fuzhou branches of the Central, China, and Communications Banks, the Minhou County Chamber of Commerce, and key members of the Provincial Government as members of the Financial Relief Committee for the Provincial Capital of Fujian. The committee held its inaugural meeting on January 5 and began working in the Minhou County Chamber of Commerce. The terms for mortgage loans are in accordance with the provisions of the outline of measures promulgated by the Provincial Government as follows: 1. Financial relief will use real estate as collateral, temporarily limited to houses and shops. Real estate valued at 2 million yuan can be mortgaged for 1 million yuan. 2. The value of the aforementioned real estate will be reviewed and evaluated by the committee collectively. A. Those who borrow from the Provincial Bank through the silver and money industry and then lend to various merchants. B. Those who borrow directly from the Provincial Bank by various merchants. C. Those with special circumstances who are approved by the committee to borrow from the Provincial Government. 3. The total amount of loans mortgaged by the silver and money industry in the provincial capital shall be limited to 300,000 yuan. The amount of direct mortgages by each merchant shall be between 500 yuan and 5,000 yuan. 4. The mortgage interest rate is set at 9% per month. 5. The mortgage period is six months. Those who repay within six months may calculate interest on a monthly basis and redeem the collateral at any time. If repayment is not possible by the due date, it may be extended for another six months at the latest. If repayment is still not possible, the committee may auction off the mortgaged real estate to compensate. The above are all the requirements for mortgage loans. As for the silver and money industry or various merchants who want to implement mortgages, they must bring the real estate deeds to the association starting on January 9, fill out the forms according to the prescribed procedures, and the association will send personnel to investigate and assess the price, and then return the deeds to the individuals. If it is considered to be within the scope of mortgage lending, the borrower can take the deeds together with the certificates issued by the association to the Fujian Provincial Bank to negotiate the loan procedures. (January 8th)

Anxi Mining Exploration Begins 91

Seventeen Japanese Technicians Depart by Land and Water: Main Target is the Geography and Overview of Pantian

Xiamen Communication: The Anxi Iron Ore Exploration Engineering Office, organized by the Construction Department of the Fujian Provincial Government, with Director Zhao Xiujin, Deputy Director Lin Zhaojin, technicians Li Qishan, Chen Zilong, Chen Yingjie, and seventeen Japanese technicians from the South Manchuria Railway Company, gathered in Xiamen in late December. Because the Full Steel Chui Mine Diamond Drilling Machine, which was rented from Mantetsu, was transported to Xiamen by the Songshan Maru, it was not taken out of customs until the end of the year, so it did not depart before the New Year. On January 3, the harbor portion was led by Lin Zhaojin and Chen Yingjie, leading Japanese technicians Soma Hideo, Igarashi Daisuke, and Yoshida Hitoshi, departed via waterway, taking the route through Zhangzhou, up the Jiulong River, inspecting water conservancy, hydropower, and harbors along the way, via Hua'an to Zhangping. Zhao Xiujin, Li Qishan, Chen Zilong, etc., led the drilling, surveying, and railway engineering Japanese technicians Kanyao Seiji, Asano Masatora, Sato , Tsuboi Mitsugu, Aratani Kazuo, Sakamoto Shuneo, Tayano Tetsuo, Isohata Sokuro, Nakagawa Kikamatsu, Matsuda Kamezo, Nakayama Takao, Otani Koichi, Yonehana Hiroshi, and Ishida Kiyoshi, and more than twenty clerks and others, set off on the morning of the 7th, crossing Jimei from Xiamen, taking three special cars, and transporting machines to depart, taking the route through Tongan into Anxi, and starting work in divisions. This Anxi mining exploration mainly targets Pantian, because its iron ore is the most abundant, the ore quality is excellent, and it has the value of large-scale mining. According to the investigation, Pantian is 140 li from Anxi County, and the Tongxi road can reach the county seat. From the county seat to Houtou is 60 li, then to Changkeng is 50 li, and then to Pantian is 30 li, all of which require walking. Pantian has two Lianbao, the Fourth Lianbao with 111 households and 521 people, and the Ninth Lianbao with 12 households and 487 people, with only a thousand people, under the jurisdiction of the Changkeng District Office. The economic organization is extremely immature. Except for food, which can be self-sufficient, everything else depends on external assistance. The people's knowledge is simple and the culture is backward, but the iron ore reserves are very rich, and the surface iron ore seedlings are visible everywhere. In addition to this, the only products are wood, bamboo, vegetables, rice, etc. It is surrounded by mountains on all sides, and the transportation is very inconvenient. The stream water is still good. The Anxi waterway can reach Zhangping in the southwest. The engineering personnel, therefore, traced the Jiujiang River to Zhangping, and inspected whether there is a place to set up hydropower along the way for iron smelting. The security of the mining exploration is protected by a large team of the 5th Security Regiment, because Anxi was previously known for its many bandits. (January 8th)

According to a tip-off, the investigation team of the Public Security Bureau learned that Li Jinxiang, the main culprit in the previous robbery of cars and weapons, had led his accomplices back to his hometown to plot wrongdoing. Jiading

Construction of the Ring Road Begins

The county government, in accordance with the order of the Construction Department of the Provincial Government, is preparing to build the South Gate to East Gate ring road for automobiles, connecting the Xihu and Jiahhu roads. The total length of the road is 2.8 kilometers, and its drawings and budget have long been approved. The cost of earthwork for the road surface is 3,255 yuan, which is contracted and undertaken by the Heji Construction Company. Construction started yesterday. The county government has ordered the people to automatically move all obstacles such as houses and tombs on the road. As for the bridge project, the budget is 14,000 yuan, and the road surface paving with sand and gravel is budgeted at 8,000 yuan. Bids are currently being designed.

Suzhou

Enclosing Lake Fields Resurfaces

In the Dongtai Lake area bordering Wuxian and Wujiang counties, a large number of migrant people enclosed the lake to form fields last year, amounting to more than 100,000 mu, which greatly harmed the lakeside farmland in Jiangwu counties. The farmers unanimously opposed it, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government sent officials to Suzhou to investigate. Together with the two counties, they sent a large number of security teams to armed enforce the enclosing and disperse the migrants, restoring the fields to the lake. Unexpectedly, those migrants, seeing the great profit, were still unwilling to give up. Recently, some people are still filling in the gaps that were removed, which was discovered by the Wujiang County Government. In addition to sending personnel to conduct on-site investigations, they also reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs and Construction. At the moment, the provincial government has dispatched Huang Yun to Suzhou to investigate. After Huang arrived in Suzhou, he took a boat to Dongshan in Dongting on the morning of the 9th and transferred to Dongtai Hunan Ku to investigate. He will go to Wujiang again tomorrow to investigate the lakeside fields in the jurisdiction of Wujiang. On the other hand, the Department of Civil Affairs and Construction has instructed the Wujiang and Wuxian county governments to earnestly crack down.

In the Dasong Fentou blood case outside the South Gate, the deceased Lin Jinsheng suffered a total of five knife wounds, which was verified by the court. Now it is known that there are surprising new developments in this case. It turns out that the deceased's wife, Chen A'da, is naturally romantic and does not abide by the virtues of a wife, repeatedly engaging in adultery. In the autumn of this year, she once attempted to murder her husband but failed. This murder case is highly suspicious. Therefore, Lu Zhenru, the head of the 20th Jia of the 3rd Bao in Lihua Town, escorted Chen A'da to the 6th Branch of the Public Security Bureau under his jurisdiction for investigation. After Duan Qishan, the chief of the branch, held a preliminary trial, according to Lin Chen's (ie, Chen A'da) confession, she was seventeen years old. Lin Jinsheng is my husband. He was recruited into my family at the age of fourteen. I lived with Jinsheng at the age of fifteen, and we never formally held a wedding. Around July of this year, while living in Zhouzhuang, I was forced to commit adultery by Lin Senbao, the cousin of Jin Quan. Later, I was instigated by Senbao to attempt to murder Jinsheng with a rope, but I failed. I then went to Suzhou and came to Wuxi on November 13. On the 4th of this month, Jinsheng said that he was going to the countryside to Liyuan to visit his brother Hesheng and was unexpectedly killed, etc. When the woman confessed, she showed no sign of grief, and Chief Duan checked the case lightly and did not pay attention to it. He did not instruct employees to record the confession. After the interrogation, he ordered the head of the Jia, Chen Zhenru, to take Lin Chen back for custody. On the morning of the 9th, Chen Jia sent her to the Public Security Bureau for investigation, so that the truth of the murder case could be revealed.

Changzhou

Telegraph Request to Exchange Copper Coins for Legal Tender

After the Ministry of Finance reformed the currency system, hard currency gradually disappeared in Wuyi City, and silver coins also decreased day by day, while copper coins were in surplus. Stores received a large number of copper coins, which could not be exchanged for legal tender for a while, and it was impossible to purchase goods without legal tender, which affected financial circulation. The County Chamber of Commerce reported the above situation based on reports from various industries, stating that it was closely related to commerce and finance. They also found that the Ministry order had issued a general order that people holding silver and copper coins could exchange them for legal tender at the nearest Central, China, and Communications banks. However, the local branches of the Middle Traffic Bank had not complied because they had not received orders from the head office, which inevitably affected finance. Furthermore, the end of the lunar year is approaching, and the period of final settlement is crucial. They specially telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting relief.

Hangzhou

Freight Car Coupling Worker Killed

Shi Hanxing, a 41-year-old freight car coupling worker from Zhuji, who had served for many years at the Hangzhou City Station, was working yesterday (9th) at 3:30 pm when the freight car was about to start. Unexpectedly, he was hit hard by the locomotive, and his left arm was broken and his chest was seriously injured. He was sent to the railway hospital for treatment, but he died at about 4 o'clock. He has five or six children behind him, and the railway bureau will provide compensation.

Foreign Banks All Agree to Hand Over Cash 96

According to the North China Daily News, it is learned that foreign banks in Shanghai have agreed to comply with the banking regulations promulgated by the Chinese government on November 4 last year, and hand over the cash they hold to the Chinese government. This decision was not made by a meeting of foreign banks, but by each bank negotiating terms with the Chinese government separately. Those who have now agreed to hand over the cash include HSBC, British Bank, Chartered Bank, Chase Bank, American Express Bank, Mercantile Bank, Banque de l'Indochine, Banque Belge pour l'Etranger, Netherlands Trading Society, Citibank. Other banks are expected to negotiate handover methods within a few days. It is heard that some banks are not yet implementing the handover, and will first report the amount of their reserves to the Chinese government in detail, and receive a receipt. Most banks handing over cash will do so with 60% cash and 40% securities, exchanged for legal tender at 100 yuan. It is heard that the Chinese authorities have begun investigating the amount of foreign currency deposited by Chinese people in foreign banks, in order to convert it into legal tender. The total amount of these deposits is more than 20 million yuan.

Bank of Communications Adds Trust Deposits 97

The Bank of Communications in this city has a special trust department, managing real estate, buying and selling securities, safekeeping important items, and acting as an agent for receiving and paying for goods, debts, and tuition fees, etc., for many years. Its business has always been developed. It is learned that the bank is now planning to add trust deposits, divided into ordinary trusts and special trusts, both to be handled by the Shanghai head office and its branches in this city first. The branches in other cities will also be promoted in order. The main points of the method are described below: Ordinary trust deposits are in the nature of agency management, with flexible terms and simple procedures. The amount of each deposit is at least 50 yuan in national currency. After one year of deposit, it can be withdrawn and used at any time. The income earned, if calculated within an annual interest rate of 6.5%, will all be enjoyed by the depositor. If it is outside of 6.5%, then the excess part will be divided equally between the bank and the depositor. Special trust deposits are for the agency of depositors' direct investment. The amount for each deposit is at least 5,000 yuan. The term and scope of use are all freely designated by the depositor. All the net profits earned, after the bank deducts a very small handling fee, belong to the depositor. There is less cost of consumption, and no labor of employing management, while enjoying stable investment benefits. It is heard that the purpose of the bank's handling of trust deposits this time is to use the bank's experience and strength to gather deposits that tend to speculate in society and use them in the path of production. Compared with private operation, it is safer and can save floating expenses. It is indeed a good way out for those in society with surplus capital. It is also known that the bank has been approved by the Ministry of Finance to allocate 2.5 million yuan in national currency as the trust department's operating fund in order to expand the trust business. All trust property accounts are completely open in order to protect the interests of depositors.

After Sanctions Against Italy, German Shipping Business Booms 99

Our country has implemented economic sanctions against Italy, restricting Chinese goods going to Italy, and also implementing a ban on the unloading of Italian goods transported to China. Our recent North German Company's express liners have seized this once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Not only is the freight traffic coming and going crowded, but there are even more passengers, and the fares have already skyrocketed. The details are recorded below:

The Italian Goods Problem

According to the Jianghai Customs announcement of sanctions on the trade of goods to and from Italy, it has been limited that imported goods from Italy to Shanghai that arrive in Shanghai after the first of this month will not be allowed to be unloaded. Subsequently, the Jianghai Customs announced its second decision, and received the revised measures for sanctions on Italian goods from the Central Ministry of Finance. If goods ordered and shipped in December of last year can still be extracted. Therefore, the goods from the Sumatara vessel from Italy to Shanghai yesterday can still be extracted. There is also the cargo ship Hilda, which will arrive in Shanghai on the 25th of this month, because most of the goods it carries left Italy before December 3, and can also be extracted as usual. However, those that depart this month and arrive in Shanghai next month will be subject to the restrictions of sanctions.

German Ships Develop

The North German Company specially built three fast ships last year, originally to compete with Italian mail ships on the Central European route. Since the maiden voyages of the two new ships, Xianghuosituo and Bosidan, the cargo and passenger businesses have still not been as good as the Italian ships. When the League of Nations sanctioned Italian goods, Italian mail ships sailing to the Far East had already suffered an invisible blow. The North German Company's express liners then flourished, and the number of cargo and passengers coming and going suddenly increased. The third new ship "Na Aisi Nu" has not yet been completed, and North Germany has already chartered the "Stuttgart" mail ship, which runs on the Atlantic Ocean, to come to China for a temporary voyage. A telegram was received yesterday, saying that it can arrive in Shanghai on the 17th of this month, and both cargo and passengers are full, and the business is better than expected.

Fare Increases

When North Germany built three special express ships for the Far East, the first-class cabin fares were priced low. Therefore, the price for traveling from Shanghai to Marseille was set at £102. Now that foreign exchange is more expensive, it has invisibly increased by one-tenth. Recently, due to sanctions against Italy, the passengers on North German mail ships leaving Shanghai for Europe have pre-purchased tickets for three or four months later, and the price has also increased to £110. The prices of other ports and second-class cabins have also increased by £4 across the board. As for round-trip tickets, they have increased by more than £10, which will be implemented starting from the postal ships exported from Shanghai this month.

The Chamber of Commerce Submits Another Request to the Ministry of Industry to Expedite Industrial Control 100

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry yesterday urging the implementation of industrial control, saying, "Respectfully submitting a request. The case is that in April of the 24th year of the Republic of China, this association, in order to save the decline of industry, should control production to avoid surplus manpower, and drafted 16 articles of regulations for control, and submitted them to your ministry for adoption. However, since it has not been approved for a long time, on August 23, a document was submitted to urge it. On September 6 of that year, your ministry issued a reply No. 13241, stating, 'The submission has been received. The implementation of industrial control is of great importance to the entire future of industry in our country. This department has long given it serious consideration. The draft regulations on industrial control submitted by the association have been studied together, and the governments of various provinces and cities have been notified to reply. Once they are collected and deliberated, and a concrete plan is obtained, they will be ordered to comply.' The association sees your ministry's care in planning the beginning, consulting widely, and not tiring of seeking details. However, the discussion of industrial control in recent years has arisen due to the needs of the environment. If Jin and Yue have already established regulations, it is better for your ministry to coordinate the overall situation and adapt to the national conditions, rather than the provinces governing themselves, which will cause more obstacles. The opinions of the provincial officials may differ, and building a house on the road may accelerate the collapse of the entire industry. It is also not the grand intention of the state to pay attention to economic construction and plan the foundation of the country. Together, we submit a sincere document and request that your ministry review it, and swiftly approve and implement it for the sake of public convenience.

Please Carefully Investigate the Cash Confiscation Case; The Ministry of Finance Replied to Yu Qiaqing Yesterday by Telegram 101

Orders have been issued to military and police agencies in various places to comply; if there are deliberate violations, the people should be allowed to accuse them

Mr. Yu Qiaqing, previously, after the Ministry of Finance implemented currency reform, the people in the interior may not fully understand the methods of exchanging legal currency. Therefore, there were times when ignorant villagers brought a small amount of cash to Shanghai to shop, but they were confiscated and fined by the military and police. The villagers mostly contained their grievances. Therefore, on the 23rd of last month, he telegraphed Chairman Chiang and the Ministry of Finance, requesting them to issue a general order to the military and police in various places to handle the matter with caution. Yesterday, he received a reply telegram from the Ministry of Finance, which said, "Shanghai Ningbo Fellow Association forwarded to Mr. Yu Qiaqing for appreciation, thanks to your request, please see, after checking, since the implementation of legal currency, in addition to the methods of exchanging legal currency promulgated by this department, it also sent letters to the three banks of China, China, and Jiaotong, and the Post Office General Bureau to sign a contract for exchanging legal currency on behalf of the other, that all postal agencies can exchange legal currency on behalf of them, so that the exchange will be universal and convenient for merchants and people. It was secretly reported that the military and police in various places failed to understand the intention of the law, and often took the opportunity to make things difficult for the ignorant people carrying a small number of coins. The above-mentioned situation should be urgently corrected at the end of the year. On the 7th day of December of last year, this department telegraphed to all provinces and cities and military agencies across the country, ordering the military and police in various places, for people in areas where legal currency is not circulating to carry silver coins to buy goods, if it is indeed not for profiteering, they should not be confiscated at will, but should order the recipient to send it to the nearest exchange agency to exchange for legal currency. The ignorant people who do not understand the policy and carry silver coins should immediately be instructed to exchange them for legal currency at the nearest exchange agency. Those who carry them to the exchange agency to exchange legal currency should not be intercepted on the way, causing disturbances. If there are deliberate violations, the people should be allowed to accuse them and be severely investigated. If they deliberately conceal, attempt to leak, or collect, transport, and operate for private profit, once detected, they should still be severely punished according to law, in order to combine compassion with the intention of preventing abuse. Sincerely hope you will check it for the sake of He, Finance Ministry Geng Qian Yin."

The Former Crown Prince of Spain Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday; Scheduled to Take a Ship to Hong Kong Tomorrow 102

The former Spanish fifth storage Giade Babang, in October last year, together with his new wife, Princess Orléans, and Viscount Rokamoli, set off from Rome, Italy, for a honeymoon trip around the world, passing through the United States, Canada, and Japan to China. First, they traveled through Beiping and Tianjin in North China, and now they have arrived directly in Shanghai by the Ping-Hu train at 7:40 AM yesterday morning. The officials in the Spanish Consulate General in Shanghai did not entertain them because it was a private trip and they were a deposed royal family. Mr. Jia plans to stay in Shanghai for two days and is scheduled to take the French Postal Ship Company's Antelibong wheel tomorrow, leave Shanghai for Hong Kong, and transfer back to Europe. Jia is the third son of the former King Alfonso. Because his two brothers gave up the inheritance, he became the crown prince. He is now 23 years old. At the age of 18, he and his parents separately fled the country. After several twists and turns, the whole country finally reunited in Paris.

The Huainan Railway is Completed; The Floating Pier Was Built by the Yongwu Factory 103

Scheduled to be shipped from Shanghai to Yuxikou for installation on the 18th

The Huainan Railway of the National Government Construction Committee, from Datong Coal Mine to Yuxikou, is 228 kilometers long. Except for the section from Datong Coal Mine to Chaoxian, which has already been opened to traffic, the section from Chaoxian to Yuxikou has been completed and opened to traffic on the 3rd, and passenger tickets will be officially sold soon. As for the Yuxikou floating pier, which was contracted by the Shanghai Yongyuan Machinery Factory, it is 300 feet long and 30 feet wide, and the cost is 80,000 yuan in national currency. It has been completed and is now moored in the Huangpu River. It is approved to be transported to Yuxikou for installation on the 18th. In the future, all the coal produced by the Datong and Huainan coal mines will be transported by this road to Yuxikou, and then transferred to Shanghai by ship.

Hosting Banks to Negotiate the Contract

Railway Bureau and Telephone Bureau Contract for Telephones at the South Station; Extended from the 24th Year to the 29th Year; Can Be Extended with Mutual Agreement Upon Expiration 106

After the Shanghai North Station was commercially equipped with public telephones by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, it has been gradually extended to Nanjing, Wuxi, Zhenjiang, Hangzhou, Ningbo, and other stations. Now, it has negotiated with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau for a contract for additional telephone sales outlets at Shanghai Station. A reporter from the Xinxin News Agency controlled and recorded its main points as follows:

Approved Methods

This contract is in accordance with the temporary measures for the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications to approve the provision of public telephone locations at stations along the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines, and these measures will be used as an attachment to this contract. With the consent of the Railway Bureau in accordance with the regulations of the above-mentioned methods, the Telephone Bureau will use the left and right locations inside the front door of the waiting hall of the Shanghai South Station as designated by the station for the Telephone Bureau to set up public telephone retail outlets. However, when necessary, the Railway Bureau may notify and designate a replacement location at any time, and the Telephone Bureau must immediately comply. The telephone set and the manager's office must be separately equipped with wooden pavilions by the Telephone Bureau. The temporary wooden pavilions are set to three, and the style, material, and paint color of the wooden pavilions must be drawn and sent by the Telephone Bureau for approval by the Railway Bureau before construction can begin. All appliances and lighting in the wooden pavilion are provided by the Telephone Bureau itself. If wooden pavilions are added in the future, they must still be handled in accordance with the various clauses of this contract.

Supply of Location

The location supplied by the legacy book telephone bureau will not be charged rent, and the telephone bureau will follow the reciprocal measures in the fifth article of the provisional methods for providing public telephone locations at stations along the railway line. The public telephone will be managed by the telephone bureau itself, or it will be managed by merchants, and the telephone bureau will notify the railway bureau of the number and names of the managers at any time for record, and all shall be handled in accordance with the fourth article of the provisional methods for providing public telephone locations at stations along the railway line. The collection of telephone charges at the retail outlet shall be handled in accordance with the seventh article of the provisional methods for providing public telephone locations at stations. This contract shall be valid from November 5, the 24th year of the Republic of China, to November 4, the 29th year. It may be extended with mutual agreement upon expiration.

The Rent Reduction Committee Petitions the Court to Temporarily Suspend the Execution of Rent Arrears Seizure, in Order to Avoid Social Panic Due to the Approaching Year-End Settlement 109

The Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee, considering that the year-end settlement period is approaching, and that there are many rent dispute cases in this city, petitioned the Jiangsu Local Court and the First and Second Special District Local Courts yesterday, requesting a temporary suspension of execution, stating that if provisional seizures are initiated, it will inevitably cause social panic. The original petition stated: "To the esteemed courts, since the Shanghai Incident, Shanghai has suffered tremendous trauma, coupled with years of drought and floods, turning villages into ruins. The rural economy has collapsed, and the social economy is showing signs of disintegration. Factories and shops have closed down one after another, and unemployed workers are wandering aimlessly. Although some are struggling to survive, many are outwardly strong but inwardly weak. Therefore, rent arrears lawsuits have arisen. Real estate that was once priced at exorbitant levels is now without buyers. Therefore, to maintain Shanghai's society, the only option is to appeal for rent reduction, which is appropriate in terms of both human sentiment and legal principles. However, people are motivated by self-interest, and landlords who are unaware of the situation are unwilling to voluntarily reduce rent. As a result, tenants are forced to default on rent, leading to dozens of rent lawsuits every day. While the judges of the court enforce the law and handle cases, the execution of provisional seizures is intended to promote the creditors' rights of the property owners. However, as the year-end settlement period is rapidly approaching, most of the industries and businesses in Shanghai are at risk of provisional seizure. Our committee, witnessing this situation, resolved at its 20th meeting to petition your esteemed courts to handle rent dispute cases with leniency, in order to help them weather this difficult situation. This matter concerns the rectification of social stability and tranquility, and we respectfully request your special attention and consideration."

The Chamber of Commerce Instructs on the Doubtful Points of Sticking Stamps on Receipts and Bills of Lading 113

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter in reply to the China Express Transportation Company, instructing that receipts and bills of lading should be stamped separately, stating: "In reply to your letter of the 8th of this month, stating that the temporary receipt issued by your company to the consignor is a temporary substitute for the bill of lading and does not seem to require stamping in accordance with the law, and requesting a letter to the Tianjin Local Court for interpretation and assistance, etc., we have found that the receipt of goods is listed in Article 16, Section 2 of the Stamp Tax Law, which is a voucher issued by the consignee to the consignor, and the bill of lading issued by the forwarding company is listed in Article 16, Section 13 of the Stamp Tax Law, which is a voucher issued by the consignor to the carrier for the extraction of goods. Their nature is different, their tax rates are different, and their effects are different. Your letter states that it is a temporary substitute for the bill of lading, and you want to invoke the temporary substitute note in Section 14 of the same article to exempt it from stamping. However, there are four prerequisites: 1. The temporary note for insurance, if it has the effect of compensation, can be used as a substitute for the insurance policy. Can this temporary goods receipt be used to extract goods and have the effect of a temporary substitute for the bill of lading? However, the receipt states that it is limited to five days to exchange for the bill of lading, and it will be invalid after the expiration date. Therefore, this receipt does not seem to be able to be used to extract goods and serve as a substitute for the bill of lading, and the so-called temporary substitute for the bill of lading in your letter also seems to be unfounded. 2. Since it is called a temporary goods receipt, does your company also have a so-called formal goods receipt, or is the so-called formal goods receipt the bill of lading? This level should also be clearly analyzed. If there is a formal goods receipt, please show us a sample. 3. If this temporary goods receipt can indeed replace the bill of lading for extracting goods, it is the same voucher as mentioned in Article 8 of the Stamp Tax Law and has two or more properties. However, because the tax rate for goods receipts is higher, it should still be stamped according to the tax rate for goods receipts. 4. If this temporary receipt cannot be used to extract goods, and the so-called formal receipt is the bill of lading, then our association believes that the receipt is one matter and the bill of lading is another, and they should be stamped separately."

The Social Bureau Organizes Statistics on Factory Worker Injuries and Illnesses, Hosting Representatives from Various Hospitals This Afternoon 114

Factories are densely packed in this city. In addition to assisting the fire department and the public security bureau in dealing with factory water disasters, the Social Bureau has also found that a considerable number of workers suffer injuries or various occupational diseases while working in factories. This matter is of great importance to workers' health and industrial economy. While many factories report the above situations to the Social Bureau in accordance with the provisions of the Factory Law, most still conceal them, making investigation difficult. In view of this, the bureau has specially formulated investigation forms to contact major hospitals in the city, requesting that when workers come to the hospital for treatment of injuries or illnesses, they fill in the details of the injury and illness according to the form and report them daily for statistical purposes, so as to collect materials and properly plan preventive measures. It is heard that the bureau has been working on this matter since last year, and the Factory Inspection Division of the bureau, together with the Municipal Health Bureau, has scheduled a meeting with representatives of various hospitals at the Youth League at 3:00 PM this afternoon (the 10th) to discuss detailed methods. The Factory Inspectors of the Bureau, Jiang Zhiyong and Li Shude, will attend at that time.
