Japanese Residents Around Wusong are Changing to Use Japanese Gold as the Standard for Ordering Prices, This Method Was Initiated by the Industrial Association, Said to be Aimed at Avoiding Exchange Rate Losses 117

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, regarding the use of Japanese currency by Japanese residents in Shanghai, the Xin Sheng News Agency has learned that it was initiated by the Industrial Association established by Japanese residents in Shanghai. The head of the Industrial Association is Makise, the owner of the Tamaya Kimono Store. The method is to uniformly convert the prices of Japanese goods imported into our country into Japanese gold standards for sale. In the past, the sale of Japanese goods in Shanghai was based on the actual value of our currency. The reason given is that it can avoid exchange rate losses. However, according to Izumi Ichinin, a spokesperson for the Japanese Embassy, ​​the Industrial Association submitted an application to the Japanese Consulate for approval, but the consulate did not agree. Although some Japanese residents in the Wusong Road area are already using this method, it is believed that it will have no effect and will stop. As for the rumors that a kind of paper money will be issued to replace cash, that is not the case. Currently, the common currency among Japanese merchants is purely Japanese gold, paper money printed by domestic banks, and Chinese legal tender.

Zhonghua Chemical Industrial Society Manufactures Glucose Products 118

Sugar is a major import commodity for our country. In recent years, the domestic chemical industry has gradually developed. The Zhonghua Chemical Industrial Society on Changan Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, has hired a German chemical PhD to manufacture glucose syrup (also known as refined sugar). It is completely refined using chemical techniques. The quality is pure and superior, far exceeding imported products, and the price is especially cheap. The reporter believes that the society's products are the pioneer of domestic products, and after more than a year of research, excellent results have been achieved. It is considered an outstanding achievement in the promotion of domestic goods. A visit was made to the factory, and its machinery purchased from Germany is quite sophisticated. It is heard that the society can produce more than 4,000 pounds of glucose per day and 130,000 pounds per month, and is sold exclusively to various confectionery companies in this city as raw materials, which is truly a high-quality domestic product. Because many places outside Shanghai have correspondence orders to promote business, and also operate their own starch factories, business is unusually developed.

45 Lawyers Who Are in Arrears with Membership Fees Will Be Reported for Expulsion if They Do Not Pay 120

The Shanghai Bar Association issued a notice to members in arrears with membership fees, stating: "Article 8, Paragraph 1, Item 7 of the Association's Provisional Rules states that members who have not paid regular fees for four months and have not paid after being notified by letter may be reported for expulsion after a resolution by the Executive Committee of the Association. There are now 45 members, including Ma Junshuo, Zhu Zhangbao, Zhou Bingyang, Yi Qifeng, Zhang Jiasheng, Fei Qiang, Du Zuomin, Cai Jue, Wu Qihua, Li Haopei, Yao Xichen, Xu Zhuan, Qu Shiji, Pang Guanyan, Chen Guanghuang, Zhou Xiaobo, Liu Liang, Ye Dahao, Huang Su, Qian Shoujia, Xia Zukun, Sun Side, Shi Baixiu, Cai Jin, Chen Boying, Wang Shaoji, Lu Tianhen, Du Yusu, Chen Wen, Gu Kenfu, Ji Yi, Wu Lidong, Xie Zhu, Zhang Chenglin, Wang Luxiang, Wang Wenmo, Chen Ding, Chen Defu, Meng Tingben, Wu Xudan, Xue Jiguang, Chen Guangyu, Kang Xuanyi, Chen Daqi, and Hu Rihua, who have been in arrears with membership fees for many months and have repeatedly failed to pay despite reminders. The 214th joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Association resolved to publish a public notice, and to limit each member to clear the payment within two weeks. If they fail to do so, they will be reported for expulsion in accordance with the regulations. This notice is hereby published. It is hoped that the overdue fees will be cleared on schedule to avoid delays. This is the notice, January 10, 1936."

Shanghai Great World Department Store to Open at 10 AM Today 123

The Great World Department Store, located between Nanjing Road, Xizang Road, and Lloyd Road, has been under preparation and construction for more than a year. Now that it is completely completed and arranged, it will open for business at 10:00 AM today. The company uses science, is well-equipped, and offers exquisite and inexpensive Chinese and Western goods. As today is the first day of business, customers are bound to be crowded. Therefore, in order to ensure the comfort of customers, the company has decided to issue a kind of exchange coupon, each coupon being worth four jiao. Admission to the venue will be by coupon, and goods can be exchanged for the coupon. The thoughtfulness for customers is evident.

Cai Changjun, the General Manager of the Shanghai Great World Company, sent a letter to Mayor Wu, stating, "When opening the business, it was originally intended to slightly arrange Qingming tea to thank all relatives and friends for their patronage and to provide guidance. However, due to the national difficulties and the frequent disasters and famines, we have respectfully saved the funds for tea and cigarettes and transferred them to charity. The board of directors has resolved to donate 3,000 yuan of national currency, requesting that 1,500 yuan be allocated to the Shanghai Fundraising Committee for Flood Relief in Various Provinces, and the remaining 1,500 yuan be allocated to various charitable organizations at your discretion. Although we know that a drop in the bucket is of no help, our humble intention will be appreciated by you." After receiving the letter, Mayor Wu distributed the original funds according to the letter and expressed his admiration for the company's enthusiasm for charity, and has sent a special letter of thanks in reply.

Resolutely Oppose Secretly Adding Transportation Fees, Fresh Meat Industry Held a Meeting Yesterday, Agreed on Methods for Pig Transportation Fees 124

According to the Da Gong News Agency, more than 1,000 fresh meat businesses in the Shanghai International Settlement have been in dispute with the Su Xi, Ren Yuan, Ning Hai, and Ning Hu slaughtering companies over the secret addition of transportation fees for several months, and the matter has not yet been resolved. It is learned that the industry convened its fourth industry representative meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss methods. More than 30 representatives, including Fan Deyu, Chen Longhu, and Huang Qixun, attended. Chairman Sun Hongyang reported on the progress of negotiations on transportation matters, and then the following resolutions were passed: 1. The transportation fee shall be 1.6 jiao per pig. 2. A subsidy of 4 fen for the company's management fee and 1 fen for circle fee. 3. A subsidy of 1 fen for the preparation of the industry association branch fee. 4. The above methods shall be officially implemented after obtaining the consent of the pig traders, the four companies, and the truck companies. 5. Before the contract is signed, all payments stopped by the truck company to the four companies should be collected by our industry. 6. Zhang Rongxin Truck Company claims that 1.6 jiao cannot be loaded and transported, and the pig traders should be notified to stop and hire other trucks to take over, otherwise it will not be recognized. The industry also sent a letter to the four companies yesterday, stating, "Dear Sirs, it has been resolved by the industry representative meeting that, regarding pig transportation matters, a contract will be jointly signed by the four parties of the pig traders, the four companies, and the truck companies, starting from February 1st. The method stipulates that the loading fee per pig is 1.6 jiao (formerly 2 jiao paid by the pig traders), with the remaining 4 fen subsidized to our industry for the preparation of the industry association branch fee in accordance with the law by 1 fen, the company's management fee by 1 fen, and a reduction of 2 fen on the industry's ticket. This principle should be agreed upon by all parties before a formal signing is scheduled. If the four companies cannot agree, then the three parties will sign, as it has no great relationship with the four companies."

Special District Rickshaw Pullers Clash with Mutual Aid Society Yesterday Morning, Over Twenty Injured and Over Thirty Arrested, Two Mutual Aid Society Executives Beaten and Property Vandalized 126

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, special district rickshaw pullers clashed with the Mutual Aid Society yesterday morning while seeking relief. Over twenty people were injured, and over thirty were arrested. The Rickshaw Pullers Association has petitioned the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other organizations and will petition Party and government organs again today. Unemployed rickshaw pullers are venting their anger everywhere, blocking and stopping rickshaws. It is possible that rickshaws may disappear from the Public Concession today. The details, as investigated by a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, are as follows:

Clash Erupts

At 9:15 yesterday morning, over five hundred rickshaw puller representatives from the five districts arrived at the entrance of the Mutual Aid Society on Jiaxing Road. Over fifty representatives entered to negotiate with the Director-General, Zhang Dengying. Zhang Dengying happened to be at the meeting handling affairs when a conflict suddenly erupted with other members of the crowd. According to the rickshaw pullers, "We came to the society to request the following: With the New Year approaching, leaseholders in previous years were able to borrow New Year's expenses. This year, due to market conditions, we were unable to borrow. We heard that the Mutual Aid Society had small loans available, so we came to request a loan. Due to the poor harvest year, we requested a three-month exemption from Mutual Aid Society fees. We wanted to borrow the auditorium to commemorate Yang Baoshan, but not only were we refused, but we were also violently beaten." However, according to the Mutual Aid Society, the rickshaw pullers, without regard for right or wrong, immediately started hitting people.

Notice on the Wall

At the same time, a notice was posted on the wall of the Mutual Aid Society's office, which read: "Workers, our business is bad, the New Year is approaching, and expenses are high. We asked the boss to borrow money, but he refused. Therefore, today we will borrow New Year's expenses from the Mutual Aid Society. If they don't agree, we will only not pay the society fees for three months as genuine relief. If the goal is not achieved, please do not retreat."

Police Investigation

At 9:30, the Jiaxing Road police station received a report and immediately dispatched a large number of detectives to protect the area around the Mutual Aid Society, closed the iron gate of the Mutual Aid Society, and took the Director-General, Deputy Director-General, and rickshaw puller representative Dai Rugui, and others, to inquire about the truth, and ordered each to be bandaged. Zhang Dengying and Chen Chunbao were then sent to Bazilu Sanatorium for treatment. At that time, other rickshaw pullers also followed and demanded to be detained as well. The police, due to the large number of people, also closed the iron gate and prohibited rickshaw pullers from entering.

Dispersing Rickshaw Pullers

At 9:45, the Central Police Station received a report and, fearing an accident, dispatched two special police vehicles to disperse the rickshaw pullers and sent over twenty special detectives to maintain order on the scene. However, the rickshaw pullers scattered and reassembled. Except for the staff, only those authorized by the Mutual Aid Society were allowed to leave and not enter. The situation was serious. Both sides remained deadlocked until 7:00 PM, when the Rickshaw Pullers Association sent representatives to persuade them to disperse. The temporary alert was also lifted.

Separate Petitions

At 10:00 yesterday morning, the Rickshaw Pullers Association sent representative Cang Gongwen to the Chinese Ratepayers Association in the Public Concession to petition, requesting: Negotiations with the Public Works Department to release the arrested rickshaw pullers. Investigate Zhang Dengying. Hand over the criminals. The secretary, Tao Leqin, received them and replied that a formal petition was required for the chairman's consideration. At 11:00, Zhu Fengxiang petitioned Yu Qiaqing, making the same requests. Yu agreed to handle it according to the law. At 2:00 PM, Zhou Weigao petitioned the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Secretary Yan Esheng received them, agreeing to handle it fairly and advised the rickshaw pullers to disperse to avoid further escalation. At the same time, petitions were also made to the First Special District Citizens' Federation and the Nantong Fellow-Countrymen Association, etc.

Arrested Rickshaw Pullers

The arrested rickshaw pullers include Xu Qingzi, Xing Hongxi, Xing Hongyi, Dai Rugui, Zhu Xitong, Lu Deguang, Chen Shuangquan, Cang Gongsen, Luan Zhaozhao, Bao Deguang, Xu Fuchang, Ji Decai, Qi Zhenqing, Jiang Jinlin, Li Fahou, Yuan San, Xue Yuquan, Wang Yiren, Ma Taizhi, Ji Songgao, Feng Guisheng, Shu Huaquan, Han Rumu, Han Rugen, Ma Guibin, Li Yourong, Li Youfu, Li Hanjun, Li Dekun, Chen Guangbo, and others, totaling over thirty people. According to police sources, twenty-three of them are considered active members and will be transferred to the court for interrogation after instructions are received. Those with less serious involvement will be released today.

Suspension of Rickshaw Rentals

According to the head of the rickshaw owners, the Rickshaw Committee has decided to start changing licenses on January 15th. The investigation has been particularly strict recently. Rickshaw pullers who have not registered will be fined one dollar and fifty cents, and their vehicles will be detained. Those without armbands will be fined fifty cents, and those without photos will be fined fifty cents. After a part of the rickshaw pullers had the conflict with the Mutual Aid Society today, the majority of renters, owners, and pullers suspended the rental and pulling of rickshaws. It is estimated that 70% of the Shanghai South District, 60% of the Shanghai East District, 20% of the Shanghai West District, 20% of the Shanghai North District, and 20% of the Shanghai Central District did not rent out rickshaws.

Investigation of Injuries

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency conducted a special investigation and found that the following rickshaw pullers were injured: Dai Rugui (head), Lu Deguang (head), Bao Degao (waist), Ji Decai (arm), Cang Gongsen (head), Qi Zhengqing (chest), Zhu Xitong (head), Xing Hongxi (waist), Xing Hongyi (chest), Chen Shuangquan (head), Luan Zhenzhao (head), Xu Fuchang (chest), Jiang Jinlin (back), Li Fahou (head), Zhu Richang (internal injuries), Jiang Chenglong (face), Li Hongjun (head), Chen Yicai (waist), Yuan San (face), Xue Yuquan (head), Wang Yiren (waist), Ma Taizhi (head), Ji Songgao (head), Feng Guisheng (head), and Han Ruben (head). On the Mutual Aid Society side, Zhang Dengying (Director-General) was injured in the chest and head, Chen Chunbao (Deputy Director-General) was injured in the head, Hu Kangning (waist), Gu Bufan (chest), Zheng Yanbin (head), and Zhou Pengnian (a worker) was injured in the head.

Blocking

At 7:00 PM, over five hundred unemployed rickshaw pullers, to oppose the Mutual Aid Society and support the petitioning rickshaw pullers, gathered in the South City and decided to split up and block rickshaws. By 7:30, many rickshaws in the Public Concession were being deflated and stopped by these unemployed rickshaw pullers along the way. Rickshaw merchants, renters, and pullers, unable to bear the losses, decided to suspend all rentals and pulling from today until the dispute is resolved.

Petition Goals

Because the Rickshaw Pullers Association in the Special District’s application for registration of unemployed rickshaw pullers was unsuccessful, and the rickshaw pullers deflated tires and blocked member's rickshaws, it was decided that the representatives from the five districts of Southeast, Northwest, and Central would gather at 8:00 AM this morning and petition the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, and the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs on a large scale. Their goals are: (1) To negotiate with the Concession for the long-term registration of rickshaw pullers; (2) To negotiate for the Mutual Aid Society to be run by the rickshaw pullers themselves; (3) To provide relief to rickshaw pullers; (4) To ensure that similar situations do not occur in the future.

Mutual Aid Society Report

According to the Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society Headquarters, at 9:00 AM on the 9th of this month, over two hundred rickshaw pullers came to the society's tea room, claiming that the renters in the South City were not releasing vehicles and their livelihoods were not secure and requested for relief (a written note was posted in various parts of the association, and a copy is attached). At that time, the society's staff, Wang Boyin, Zhang Xiaojiang, etc., responded to them. While they were talking, Cang Gongsen, Li Yourong, Li Youfu, and others led over eighty rickshaw pullers from the Rickshaw Pullers Association, pretending to be coming to the meeting for tea. After they had securely guarded all the doors of the office, Cang Gongsen closed the main gate of the association facing Dixwell Road and guarded it himself. At the same time, over ten rickshaw pullers jumped over the inquiry counter and shouted to hit. When they swarmed into the office, the society's staff, Gu Bufan, Wang Boyin, Hu Kangning, etc., stepped forward to stop them and were all beaten. Other rickshaw pullers who only listened to one side swarmed into the meeting room. At that time, the staff of the education department, etc., tried hard to pull the door closed, but because they were not strong enough, the rickshaw pullers broke the window and burst in, and joined the rickshaw pullers who had rushed in from the office, and swarmed into the Director-General's office (there was a tall rickshaw puller guarding the telephone, his porcelain license number was 28202, and he had a yellow earring on his left ear), dragged the Director-General (Zhang Dengying) to the meeting room, pushed him down and beat him indiscriminately. Deputy Director-General (Chen Chunbao) stepped forward to dissuade them and was also dragged in and beaten. Some grabbed the supplies in the meeting room to use as weapons. At this time, the society's worker Zhou Pengnian bravely stepped forward and shielded Director-General Zhang with his body and was beaten for over ten minutes. The society's staff witnessed some of the rickshaw pullers who did it deliberately hit their faces and hands, etc. At this time, two policemen arrived. The staff of the society then called the police station to request for additional policemen, but could not do so. When Director-General Zhang and Deputy Director-General Chen saw the policemen arrived, they shouted for help. Deputy Director-General Chen even shouted loudly to the policeman next to him, "Policeman, please try to stop them!" Although there were two policemen at this time, Director-General Zhang and Chen were still being beaten. The staff of the society could not do anything because the telephone lines were not working and the front and back gates were guarded. About ten minutes later, one Western policeman and two Chinese policemen arrived and started to disperse some of the rickshaw pullers. The arsonists who beat Director-General Zhang and Chen were still extremely arrogant. Knowing that they could not escape, they claimed that they had to reason with the police station and twisted the two Director-Generals together and, under the suppression of the Chinese and Western policemen, led them to the police station. There were also some rickshaw pullers who had not yet committed the acts and then laid ambush in the various departments of the association, and for some reason, beat each other again. At this time, several Chinese, Western, and Indian policemen successively escorted the arsonist rickshaw pullers to the police station. However, many rickshaw pullers surrounding the outside of the association had tried to rush into the gate several times and were stopped by the Chinese and Western policemen left behind. At around 10:00, Wang Zhiren, a member of the Rickshaw Committee, first came to the association to investigate and, while getting into the car, was surrounded by the rickshaw pullers standing outside the association gate, preventing the car from leaving. The police dispersed them and arrested the ringleader. The injuries of Director-General Zhang and Deputy Director-General Chen still need to be examined by the hospital. However, Zhou Pengnian, a worker of the association, has been sent to Renji Hospital for examination and emergency treatment due to his serious injuries. The staff of the association with minor injuries have been treated separately by the association's clinic (Gu Bufan injured his hand and bled a lot). Up to noon on the twelfth, there were still many people in short clothes gathered around the association and did not disperse. The association had received a secret report yesterday morning, and Director-General Zhang of the association specially notified the police station by telephone, and soon after this serious and unfortunate incident occurred. The departments and items destroyed and damaged by the association have been surveyed and registered by the police several times. In order to clarify the facts, the association has attached a list of the rickshaw pullers' disturbances and losses to the rear. The original text of the rickshaw pullers' notice posted by the arsonists (already seen above, omitted). An overview of the destroyed departments of the association: Inquiry office: Eleven teapots were smashed, and more than twenty teacups were smashed. One pair of Deputy Director-General Chen's glasses were smashed, and his shoe covers were lost. Statistics room: The writing desk was overturned, the display windows were broken, books were trampled and torn, many office supplies were destroyed, and one yellow woolen hat was lost. Meeting room (兼 Education Department): The stove was knocked over, the chimney was trampled, the doors and windows were broken, many of the books distributed at the beginning of the semester were trampled and torn, the spittoon was broken, and many office supplies were destroyed. Intellectual Education Department: The net basket was trampled, books were trampled and torn, the display windows were broken, and many office supplies were destroyed.

Courtroom Listening Seats Full, Xi Yuncao Case Continues Hearing Yesterday, Xi Yunqing's Complexion Pale and Spirit Depressed, Chauffeur Frowns, Seems Regretful, Because Witnesses Were Not Present, the Court Adjourned the Continued Hearing 129

Liu Zirong, the third young son of Liu Huizhi, the former general manager of the China Industrial Bank, married Liu Xi, the daughter of Xi Exian, a Jiangyin dye merchant (also known as Xi Yunqing and Yunqing). The couple's relationship was initially harmonious, but because Liu Zirong spent less time at home, Xi Yunqing was lonely in her boudoir, which led to her being seduced by the hired chauffeur, Wu Wenxiang, and they eloped together. They hid in the kiosk at No. 84 Jixiangfang, Wujianong, Qianjiatang, in the French Concession. Liu Zirong found out, called the police, and went to the address to arrest them. Liu Xi and Wu Wenxiang were arrested and transferred by the Public Security Bureau to the Procuratorate of the District Court. After the prosecutor Tang Ruxiu's investigation was completed, Liu Xi and others were prosecuted for adultery, based on their repeated admissions at the Public Security Bureau. Judge Shao Qinzhi held a public trial that was not concluded, and the two defendants were sent back for further trial. At the same time, the lawyers of both parties were instructed to conduct reconciliation outside the court. The details have been recorded in previous reports. The District Court held a trial at 2:00 PM yesterday. At 1:00 PM, the gallery on the second floor was already full.

Early Warning of Full Seats

Those who arrived later still came in droves, but there were no seats available. They all stood on tiptoe. Judicial Sheriff Zhang Shuping was deeply concerned that too many people in the gallery would disrupt court order, so he supervised four bailiffs to take care of the court. At 2:30, Judge Shao took the bench and first heard trivial cases. Seeing the unusually crowded gallery, he ordered that the chauffeur's adultery case be heard in the first courtroom (the first and second courtrooms were the largest, with a very large area, and the gallery could accommodate hundreds of people). The audience listened to the order and crowded into the first courtroom.

Compete With Each Other

The order was slightly chaotic, but Chief Judge Pang Shurong was hearing a land appeal case in the first courtroom. It was already 3:30 when Chief Judge Pang finished the trial and left the court. Judge Shao and the clerk of court then came to the court and took the bench. The audience's spirits were lifted. The three lawyers, Chao Kun, Tu Kunfan, and Gu, hired by the first defendant, Liu Xi, and the lawyer Tong Banggan, hired by the second defendant, Wu Wenxiang, arrived in court one after another. Judge Shao ordered Liu Xi and Wu Wenxiang to be brought to the case and first ordered them to sit temporarily on the side benches. Liu Xi's

Pale Complexion

She looked around, not as red-faced and extremely shy as she was during the last court hearing. Wu Wenxiang, on the other hand, was gaunt, frowning, and silently lowering his head, as if he regretted it. The judge asked whether Liu Zirong's lawyers were present and to what extent the case had been reconciled outside the court. Lawyer Gu replied that his lawyer had repeatedly met with Shan Yuhua, the lawyer commissioned by Liu Zirong, and had some clues. He was asked about the

Terms of the Question, Answer: There are no special conditions. Today, his lawyer received a phone call from the family of Lawyer Shan, saying that Lawyer Shan had gone to Zhenjiang beforehand and had not yet returned to Shanghai. It was uncertain whether he could arrive in court today. He asked the court to change the date of the joint trial because there was a possibility of reconciliation outside the court. Then Lawyer Dong stood up and said that the defendant Wu Wenxiang in this case requested the judge to allow him to be released on bail. Then Lawyer Tu Kunfan stood up and said that the divorce case of the first defendant, Liu Xi, had been ordered by the First Special Court to expedite the reconciliation between the two parties by inviting relatives and friends within one month.

Conduct Reconciliation

However, personal lawsuits must be based on the wishes of both parties. The defendant is currently detained in your court, and all reconciliation proceedings are very difficult. Moreover, the defendant has been married to Liu Zirong for many years and has a son. If the couple remembers their past feelings, they will be closer to reconciliation. He asked the judge to allow him to be released on bail. The questioner said that the first defendant, Liu Xi, had previously submitted a statement requesting bail. Her

Reasons for Bail

It was claimed that she was ill. After a forensic examination by the court, Liu Xi was not ill. Therefore, the issue of bail will be determined when the case is concluded. He also ordered that since the defendant's lawyer had requested a change of date today, and Liu Zirong and the witnesses summoned by the court had not reported, he would be allowed to reschedule the trial. Yang Bangji and Lu Zhenmin Shot by Thugs, Five People Suddenly Opened Fire During Dinner, Yang and Lu Both Severely Wounded 130

Yang Bangji, a native of Yancheng, 36 years old, lives at No. 63, Lane 625, Mett Hess Road. He used to make a living by renting out rickshaws. At around 7:40 yesterday afternoon, Yang, his friend Lu Zhenmin, a native of Yancheng, 30 years old, and five members of his family were having dinner together when five men suddenly came outside the door, speaking with a Jiangbei accent. They broke into the inner room and, without asking why, each took out a pistol and fired four or five shots at Yang and Lu. At that time, Yang and Lu were having dinner and could not dodge in time. They were hit and fell to the ground with blood gushing out. When the murderers saw that their purpose had been achieved, they shouted and fled. When Yang's family called for help, the nearby police rushed to the scene, but the murderers had already escaped. They immediately telegraphed the Jing'an Temple Police Station, first sent a car to take the two to the hospital for treatment, and then went out to hunt down the murderers. Yang was shot in the left abdomen, injuring the large intestine. Lu was shot in the neck and left foot. All were serious injuries, so the situation was very critical. As for who the murderers were, the victims were not conscious and did not make a clear statement, only vaguely answering that some of the murderers were rickshaw pullers and some were relatives, fearing that it was due to an unsuccessful loan. The police are currently investigating.

Extortion from Xiang Yixing, Four Robbers Apprehended, One Thief Knows the Victim, All Detained for Further Investigation 131

Xiang Yixing, a native of Ningbo, 50 years old, the owner of the Xingchang Iron Factory at No. 150 O'Car Road, is quite wealthy and a devout Buddhist. He has a family temple on Gonghe Road, Zhabei, where he often goes to recite scriptures and practice Taoism. On July 20th last year, Xiang was kidnapped and a large sum of money was extorted. He escaped danger on August 18th and stayed at home, spending his days in leisure. Unexpectedly, between October 13th and January 6th this year, there were other bandits coveting him and sent ten threatening letters one after another. At first, they demanded 80,000 yuan, then reduced it to a minimum of 20,000 yuan, and arranged for someone to bring the money to meet them near the telegraph pole at No. 141 Dongjiadu, Pudong. Otherwise, they would take drastic measures. Xiang was so troubled by these people that he took the letter to the Jiaxing Road Police Station and went to the agreed location to observe the situation, but no one came to talk. At 6:30 PM the day before yesterday, Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Inspection Office, Detective Liu Shaokui, and Detectives Chen Yonggui, Qian Xianzhang, Xie Futang, etc., arrested Wei Youliang (also known as A San), a native of Chongming, Wang Jinzhang, Zhang Guangen, and Xi A Gen (also known as Changjiao A Gen), natives of Pudong, at Room 16, Jiaotong Hotel, No. 37, Lane 117, Shandong Road, and transferred them to the Jiaxing Road Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were transferred to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The lawyer of the Public Works Department, Zhu, detailed the previous situation and claimed that the last two letters were named by Zhang Desheng and Xu Jinbiao, requesting an adjournment of the case. He then submitted the threatening letters for inspection. According to the victim Xiang Yixing's statement, he was rescued by detectives from the Public Security Bureau. He did not give ransom money to the kidnappers. The only thing the defendants said was that Wei Youliang used to see him playing in the temple. When the four defendants were questioned, they confessed that the escaped leader, someone A, had initiated the idea. They admitted that they had written the last two threatening letters, but they did not know the rest. The rest of the confessions were vague. Judge Xiao Bianfen ordered them to be returned to custody and the case to be verified at a later date.

Son Makes Things Difficult for Old Father, Father Commits Suicide in Anger, Leaves Two Suicide Notes, Describing Son's Bullying 132

Zhang Ronghua, a native of Xiuning, Anhui, 55 years old, owns the Runyuan Used Clothing Store at No. 427 Minquan Road in the French Concession and has a Runcheng branch store in Kunming. He married a local woman, Zhou (40 years old this year), early in his life and lived in Sanxingli No. 93, Dapu Road, South City, in the Chinese Concession. Zhang's son from his mistress, Gui Lin, is 27 years old this year and married into the family of his fellow villager Zha Jiren as his son-in-law. Gui Lin and his father-in-law run the Dingtai Clothing Store on Lanmidu, Pudong. Zhang Ronghua owns two stores. Due to the poor market situation recently, business has been slow, resulting in huge debt losses. In October last year, his son Gui Lin transferred 300 yuan in cash and more than 200 yuan in goods, repeatedly demanding payment. Unexpectedly, Gui Lin not only refused to return them, but also colluded with hooligans to make things difficult for his father. Zhang Ronghua learned that his hatred was difficult to vent and that the year-end business summary period for merchants was approaching and could not be compensated. For these reasons, he had a negative thought. On the night of the 7th, he slept in the store and secretly swallowed raw opium to commit suicide. At 10:30 the next morning, Zhang's second son, Guan Mao (17 years old, studying in the store), saw that his father had not yet gotten up and went into the room to call him, but there was no response. He then discovered that he had committed suicide by poisoning. There was a box of raw opium left over next to his pillow, with a small amount of opium and two suicide notes inside, describing how he was bullied by his son and owed debts. He was immediately sent to Renji Hospital, but the poisoning was too deep and the treatment was ineffective. He died at 1:30 in the afternoon. The hospital reported it to the French Police Station, and detectives were sent to investigate the cause of death. The body was sent to the Tongren Garden Yuenfengtang morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Wang Ren of the Second Special District Court and forensic clerks arrived at the morgue and confirmed that the deceased, Zhang Ronghua, had committed suicide by poisoning before his death. After questioning the deceased's wife, Zhang Zhou, and second son, Zhang Guanmao, they were ordered to sign an undertaking to claim the body for burial.

Guo Futting Sued by His Eldest Son's Concubine 135

Father Takes Son's Concubine, Causes Her to Leave, Promises Money But Fails to Fulfill

Guo Futting, a wealthy businessman from Chaozhou residing at No. 4 Fu'an Lane, South Chengdu Road, was recently sued in the First Special District Court by Guo Yu, the concubine of his eldest son, Yucai, for failure to fulfill an agreed-upon debt. The grounds for the lawsuit are as follows: Guo Futting previously took Chen Lianxiang as his concubine. Chen gave birth to a son named Guan Hong in June of the 23rd year. On July 3rd of the same year, the defendant and Chen signed a contract, allocating real estate worth 200,000 yuan to Chen, with 150,000 yuan as Guan Hong's inheritance and 50,000 yuan as Chen's alimony. Subsequently, the plaintiff's aunt suspected that Chen's union with the defendant was based on the plaintiff's relationship, so she forced Yucai to separate from the plaintiff. The defendant, feeling that the plaintiff had taken the blame for him, made another agreement, allocating one-third of Chen's 50,000 yuan share to the plaintiff. However, recently the defendant regretted this and so the plaintiff filed a lawsuit, requesting the court to order the defendant to pay the plaintiff 16,700 yuan, plus interest. The case was heard yesterday afternoon in Civil Court Thirteen of the First Special District Court by Judge Wang Daxi. The defendant, Guo Futting, hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to appear in court and argue that Yu was the third concubine of the defendant's son, Yucai. Yucai had long been independent, and the defendant had no obligation to support the plaintiff. At the time, because Yu was living with the defendant's concubine, Chen, the defendant entrusted Yu to take care of Chen and gave her one-third of the living expenses paid to Chen as compensation. However, later, the defendant severed relations with Chen, so Chen's living expenses were also canceled, and the plaintiff's one-third compensation also ceased to exist. The contract was also taken back and destroyed. Chen's 50,000 yuan matter was a completely separate issue. Therefore, the plaintiff's request is completely unfounded and should be dismissed. Judge Wang, after reviewing the case, determined that further investigation was necessary and adjourned the hearing.

Giant Timber Crushes Xie Xisheng's Leg, Sues Construction Company for Injury 137

Family's Livelihood Threatened, Right to File Ancillary Civil Suit Reserved

Xie Xisheng, a native of Shaoxing residing at No. 295 Rue Galieni in the French Concession, was walking near the intersection of Xizang Road and Race Course Road at around 10:00 AM on the 9th of last month when the Yongchang Construction Company at No. 31 Longmen Road was constructing a building. Due to the negligence of the workers, a giant timber fell from the third floor, striking Xie, knocking him to the ground. His head, fingers, and left leg were injured, and he fell unconscious. A police officer arrived and sent Xie to Renji Hospital for treatment. The diagnosis revealed that his left leg bone was broken, and it was treated with a plaster cast. According to the doctor, it would take one to two years to recover. Xie's family relied entirely on his income to make a living. Due to the injury, his family's livelihood was threatened. Therefore, he hired lawyer Jia Yaoxi to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Zhou Gongshan, the owner of the Yongchang Construction Company, for negligent injury, and reserved the right to file an ancillary civil suit. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Wanchang heard the case in Criminal Court Nine. Xie Xisheng was carried to the court and described the incident. Zhou Gongshan argued that he was a "general contractor" and that the project was contracted to another party, so he was not responsible. The plaintiff's lawyer argued that the issue of "general contractor" and "subcontractor" was an internal matter for the defendant and could not be used as a reason to evade responsibility. The court determined that further investigation was necessary and adjourned the hearing. The defendant, Zhou Gongshan, was released on bail of 500 yuan to await further summons.

After receiving the report, the bureau submitted a request to the Executive Yuan's Health Department, which forwarded it to the Shandong Provincial Department of Education to verify that the graduation diploma was indeed forged. According to reliable information from the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, in view of the large number of homebound passengers during the New Year holidays, which is bound to cause crowding, in addition to the regular passenger trains running at 12:00 AM, 12:50 AM, and 5:15 AM, from January 10th to January 24th and from January 29th to February 16th, an additional special third and fourth class train, No. 48, will run daily on the Shanghai-Nanjing line from Shanghai to Zhenjiang, arriving at Shanghai North Station at 35 minutes past the hour. The railway is also providing special services for busy passengers in Shanghai. Passengers' luggage, if it does not exceed the free weight limit, can be transported by the railway from the departure station to the destination station. Shanghai Municipal Council Reopens Reconstructed Wayside Wharf 145

The Wayside Public Wharf on Yih Heung Road in the Eastern District was originally made of wood and was built in 1913. It was used for twenty years. However, due to the considerable annual repair costs and increasing usage, it was decided to rebuild it. It is now reported that the wharf has been partially reconstructed with steel and concrete by the Shanghai Municipal Council's Public Works Department and was reopened for use the other day. Since the reconstruction, the wharf is more solid than before, and the bottom of the river has been further excavated, making the water level deeper than before. All shallow-water boats and barges can now dock at the shore. There is also a crane with a maximum lifting capacity of seven and a half tons, which can be borrowed at any time for a very low fee. It is said that the original reconstruction plan for the wharf included all wharf facilities, but due to economic reasons, only the western part, which is 163 feet long, could be built first, and the reconstruction of the eastern part will have to wait until the future.

Public Concession - Industrial Accident Statistics for Last Month 152

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council, the number of industrial and occupational accidents that occurred in the Public Concession of Shanghai last December was 179, slightly less than the 188 in November. Six people died in that month, and six female workers were injured. A total of 110 of these cases were thoroughly investigated, and factory owners were given instructions on how to prevent future accidents. Of those who died, one was in the metal and machinery industry, one was in the food, beverage, and tobacco industry, one was in the textile industry, one was in the construction industry, one was in the printing industry, and one was in the transportation industry. In terms of the cause of death, three people were killed by falling objects, one was killed by machine shafts, one was killed by fire, and one fell from a height. In terms of the type of industry, 34 people were injured in the metal and machinery industry, and one died. The food, beverage, and tobacco industry had 14 accidents, with one death. The transportation industry had 22 accidents, with one death. The textile industry had 19 accidents, with one death. The construction industry had 12 accidents, with one death. The vehicle manufacturing industry had 15 accidents.

Sports Training in the Soviet Union: The Entire Nation Must Exercise; Sports Schools Are Everywhere 160

TASS Moscow, December 18th: The Soviet Union pays special attention to sports training. Moscow, Leningrad, Kharkov, and Baku all have large sports academies with a total of 4,000 students. In addition to studying scientific and natural sciences, students must also study physical education and various sports techniques. In 1934, 415 graduates were sent to various schools and enterprises as sports instructors. Many famous Soviet educators are graduates of the aforementioned schools. The Moscow and Leningrad Sports Academies received the Lenin Medal for their excellent performance.

Twenty cities in the Soviet Union have secondary sports schools, training 5,000 physical education instructors for factories and collective farms. Physical education and sports are extremely popular in the Soviet Union. This is due to the large number of young people joining sports schools. For example, this year, the Moscow Physical Education Academy enrolled 500 students, with 1,600 applicants. Kiev enrolled 200 students, with 600 applicants.

World Professional High Diving Performer Marcel Ski Commits Suicide; Driven to Extremes by Economic Pressure 164

World professional high diving performer Marcel Ski committed suicide on the 6th of this month by jumping from the eleventh floor of the Tang Tang Building in Los Angeles, California. He broke his bones and tore his skin upon landing, and died immediately. Mr. Ski was 58 years old and had created various styles, becoming the world's authority on high diving. He had traveled to the Far East many times, even performing in Manila a year ago. The reason for his suicide was economic pressure. He had recently worked as a , but then became unemployed, leading to worry and resentment that drove him to this extreme. The American swimming community deeply regrets this tragic news.

Two Major Initiatives of the Japanese Media in This Year's Sports World: Using Aircraft to Cover and Deliver News of the Berlin Olympics; Inviting Professional Tennis Players Tilden and Vines to Perform 165

(Tokyo Correspondence) The advancement of business depends solely on news, and the advancement of the news business depends solely on speed. The advancement of sports especially lies in on-site observation and technical review. In recent years, the rapid progress of the Japanese sports world has alarmed the world. In this year's Berlin Olympics in August, there is a strong call to seize championships, and the heroic words are enough to show Japan's spirit of hard work in every endeavor, which is enough to alarm our country's authorities. Here are two major sports initiatives of the Tokyo Yomiuri Shimbun in this year to inform the nation.

(1) Special Express Flight On-Site Communication of the Asian Olympics

The mobilization of modern science is a key to the rapid advancement of the news business. Such as aircraft communication, major news agencies around the world have specialized aircraft, it is not surprising. However, this Asian Olympics, is far away in Berlin, Europe, and it is commendable that a single news agency in our Asia has this great act. They have ordered the latest high-speed aircraft in Germany, called the "BFW108B model aircraft" with a speed of 300 kilometers per hour, has an endurance of eight hours. The long distance between Tokyo and Berlin is 11,000 kilometers (7,000 miles), and can be reached in just three days. This aircraft is specially prepared for the 11th Asian Olympics to deliver on-site photographs, records, and books. They all say that this long-distance air flight is still the world's latest business. This is also a record in the world's aviation history to fly day and night over the Siberian wilderness. Pilots "Kumakawa" and "Iitori Mechanic" will go to Germany on the 5th to practice the new aircraft.

(2) Recruiting American Tennis Players Tilden and Vines

Every year, the Japanese sports world invites world-class sports figures to perform in the country, is a major reason for the rapid advancement of their sports skills. Such as the past recruitment of European and American track and field teams, boxing teams, baseball teams, swimming teams, the obvious achievements, is no controversy. Now the Yomiuri Shimbun has announced the recruitment of two great tennis masters in the world, then expect other similar heroic acts, are yet to come in succession.

Tilden, 42 years old, was the United States' 11-year-old Davis Cup representative (since 1920). He continued to maintain the United States' honor in the Davis Cup for seven years. Tilden's unique serve, volley, and chop have completely broken through the European style of defense. His miraculous attack is famous in the world.

Vines, 24 years old, is a new figure in the American tennis world who has risen after Tilden. He dominated the world at the age of 20. Recently, he joined a professional tennis team, and his superb skills are improving, greatly surpassing Tilden, Pan Le (England), Crawford (Australia), Kramm (Germany), and is recognized as the world's No. 1 star.

In the cloud, Tilden and Vines won five world professional tennis titles, and after five fierce demonstration performances, their fierce serves and lightning volleys have become the unique skills of tennis, all asserted that it is the foundation for a major advancement in Japanese tennis, and these two have already telegraphed their acceptance.

Wartime Education Work Plan (6) - Colleagues of the Education Research Institute of Zhongshan University 171

6. Wartime Work Plan for Private Schools

A. Organizational System

The organizational system for wartime work in private schools takes the school-wide wartime work committee as the highest authority, with teams as the central organization and groups as the basic organization.

Children, youth, and women each form a team, with one captain and one vice-captain for each team, filled by teachers and students respectively.

Below the teams are groups, divided by work type, such as agricultural and pastoral groups, fire fighting groups, etc., each group consisting of about ten people.

Students are assigned to various groups according to their abilities, level, and address. Each group elects one representative.

Parents of students and nearby residents are welcome to participate freely.

Teachers serve as instructors for each group.

The school-wide wartime work committee is chaired by the principal and has five departments: (1) Personnel Registration Department, (2) Needs Assessment Department, (3) Skills Training Department, (4) Academic Guidance Department, and (5) Social Work Department. Each group is both a constituent of its respective team and subject to the jurisdiction of the corresponding part of the school-wide committee, to ensure the consistency of school-wide work.

The organizational chart for each level is shown below.

B. Work Outline

Teachers guide students in filling out ability and occupation survey forms.

Classify and register various wartime personnel.

Teachers go to designated areas to investigate wartime needs in various aspects. Change the original teaching time for each subject, extracting five hours per week to teach new wartime teaching materials.

The Needs Assessment Department promptly disseminates wartime news.

In addition to general activities, the implementation of work focuses on the following items: (1) militia training, (2) caring for wounded soldiers, (3) digging cellars, (4) practicing using water carts for fire fighting, (5) women making cotton clothing, (6) planting, animal husbandry, and producing food, (7) transporting military supplies and food, etc., (8) renting vehicles and boats to help refugees in war zones, (9) building roads and bridges, (10) maintaining public order, (11) using paper currency.

Each team gathers for exercises every Sunday.

In addition to government funding, the expenses required for wartime work are freely donated by faculty and students.

C. Implementation Steps

The principal convenes an emergency wartime meeting to discuss preparations for wartime work.

Teachers go to the local wartime work committee for training.

Members of the school-wide wartime work committee take an oath.

Teachers of each team promote the necessity of wartime work to students and parents.

Investigate the abilities, interests, and family occupations of all faculty, students, and staff.

Announce the names of the members of each group.

The school committee investigates wartime needs and designates each team to be responsible for meeting them.

Raise funds to purchase equipment.

Implement training.

Start working.

Preliminary Department Subject Competition at Zhengshi Middle School 172

The private Zhengshi Middle School in this city has a unique approach to student training, paying particular attention to extracurricular activities. This semester, the preliminary department held a basic science competition (i.e., Chinese, English, and Mathematics). Awards were given in two forms: group and individual. The competition methods differed between Chinese and English/Mathematics. The English/Mathematics assessment process consisted of preliminary and final rounds. The exam questions for each subject were selected by the Assessment Committee from this semester's textbooks, with ten questions chosen. First, a preliminary round was held within each grade and group (the school divides each grade into three or four groups). The group's score was calculated as a percentage of the total possible points. The group with the highest score in the grade received the group award. The top ten performers in each group's preliminary round participated in the grade-wide final round. The top three performers after the final round received individual awards. For the individual competition in Chinese, there was no preliminary round, only a competition held within each grade and group. The top three individual performers received awards. For groups, the top three groups with the highest scores received awards. It has been learned that the final round results showed that many students in each grade achieved perfect scores in English and Mathematics. The committee raised the difficulty of the questions and shortened the time limit, holding another final round to determine the award winners. According to the school's administrator, this type of competition best encourages students' interest in studying. During the competition period, which coincided with nationwide student unrest, the school's students were still working hard, neglecting sleep and meals. This is truly rare. It is said that the school held an awards ceremony on January 6, which inspired all the students.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (1) (4) (7) 174

— Original by Louisa Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"Maybe the old hen swallowed it; they are all greedy little fellows," she said; Xiao Qiao couldn't help but laugh, which ignited her anger, and she went to hit her brother, startling him. She then burst into tears, running away while shouting, "He's not! He's not! He's not!"

Her aunt and uncle were unwilling to shake the child's trust in her friend, hoping that her innocent feelings might one day prove to be correct, and therefore liked her even more. Later, after this incident passed, Nader often said that if it weren't for Xiao Mei, he simply wouldn't have been able to bear it. While others avoided him, she was unwilling to follow suit, becoming even closer to him than before. When he was comforting himself with his broken piano, she would now sit beside him and listen quietly, her face full of trust and love. At this time, Nader would completely forget his humiliation and feel very happy. She asked him to help her with her schoolwork. In her small kitchen, she cooked all sorts of food, which he would swallow wholeheartedly, no matter what it was, because gratitude could imbue even the worst taste with a fragrant aroma. When she saw that he didn't dare to play with other children, she suggested that they play baseball, team ball, etc. She picked some small flowers from her little garden and placed them on his writing desk—using all sorts of ways to show that she was not a fickle friend, and that no matter what his social status was, she would always be loyal. Nan En soon followed her lead, at least in outward appearance, so as not to embarrass others; she restrained her sharp tongue and prevented her nose, which often showed contempt, from expressing any doubt or displeasure. This was especially difficult for Mrs. Qi Tan (Note), because she firmly believed that Nader must have taken the money.

(Note) Qi Tan is a homophone for "garrulous."

Commercial News

Finance: Exchange Rate Hardens, Gold Standard Drops Another Three Yuan and Three Jiao, Market Conditions Extremely Quiet for the Day, Only Over Eight Thousand Transactions 175

The gold market was extremely quiet yesterday. The exchange market loosened, with swap rates nearing parity, leading to more selling pressure. As a result, prices continued to fall, with scattered trading within the market. Prices fluctuated only within a range of three yuan throughout the day. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets saw London rise and the U.S. remain stable. Footnotes indicated that after closing, there were a small number of off-market forward transactions at the quoted price, negotiated privately, at a discount of about 0.25 compared to spot prices, but the volume was limited. The Montreal forward silver price fell between 2.5 and 7 points. Exchange rates remained high. London spot gold remained unchanged. The Central Bank's quoted price was revealed, with both British and U.S. rates unchanged. The customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard gold standard price was still quoted at 1146.9 yuan. Sentiment was lukewarm. Off-market provisional trading opened at around 46 yuan, with very few transactions. Later, Dingtai and others made minor sales, opening lower in the morning. After the opening, banks were congested with demand, the exchange market hardened, and selling pressure was more intense, leading to continued declines. HSBC's quoted prices were revealed, with both British and U.S. rates unchanged. The situation fluctuated, with small increases, but soon retreated. Demand was extremely quiet, with small positions also slight. Prices hovered around 5 yuan. Shenbao Literary Weekly

Ah Sen and His Ox 192

— Qian Dong

It seemed to be his habitual action. When his yellowish-wax teeth were biting on that old and smooth short tobacco pipe, Ah Sen always had to shake his head, letting that long braid sway a bit, before he would desperately search inside his few ragged clothes with both hands.

A short red-headed match was fished out, struck on the ground with a "whoosh," the tobacco pipe glowed red for a moment, and then his mouth sucked forcefully. Rings of smoke followed his comfortable breath and flew out, gradually dissipating in the fields.

Now, Ah Sen sat down on the bluestone slab, and like the smoke rings flying out of his mouth, his mind also vaguely fell into deep thought.

The November sun was as warm as in the second or third month of spring, shining on the already plowed land like golden fish scales. On the uncultivated land, many sparrows chirped, pecking at the golden, desolate ears of grain. It was indeed a time very suitable for deep thought.

Ah Sen narrowed his eyes and counted the land he had already plowed. The golden fish scales were all smiling at him, and so his heart smiled as well.

"Soon, soon, only the two 'mu' and five 'fen' on the east side are left."

Suddenly, two clumsy sounds startled him. He turned his head: it was his ox, struggling clumsily and resisting the rope. He angrily knocked his smooth tobacco pipe hard on the bluestone slab, scolding loudly, "Beast! Beast! Beast! Hey! Hey!"

The beast calmed down, and he slowly thought, thought, with half-closed eyes. A murmuring, self-talking sound rumbled: "This beast, it's suffered enough with me. After plowing these two 'mu' and five 'fen', I should buy some 'flower cakes' to nourish it…"

Flower cakes? At the mention of flower cakes, he immediately thought of lace. The round cakes not only looked like lace and sounded like it; but the way the price of flower cakes kept rising day by day was truly as precious as the steadily decreasing pattern. This made his heart tighten, and he immediately felt a chill.

He put away his tobacco pipe, tied it to his belt, and walked into deep thought with even more dazed eyes.

Winter plowing is finished… flower cakes are really not important. What is important is still the three-person family's food… He thought again of his eternally miserable wife, who spent her life mending torn clothes, carrying grain sacks, carrying dung buckets, being scolded… Gradually, his thoughts turned to Ah Fu, who was cutting ox grass in the graveyard across the way. This child was also too miserable, still wearing only a single cloth shirt and pants, and snow was coming soon.

And so, he thought of borrowing grain on credit. Under the current circumstances before the New Year, it was absolutely necessary to borrow some grain on credit. If he borrowed it, he could live comfortably this year, and he would have the capital to sow next year… Old Jin Rong suddenly jumped into his mind, his rat-like eyes smiling slyly, calculating other people's property again. When the one 'dan' of grain he had squeezed from him a month ago was sold on the market, he could squeeze two 'dan'…

A startling sound interrupted his deep thought:

"Runaway ox! Runaway ox!"

It was Ah Fu and many other children cutting grass in the graveyard across the way who were shouting. Ah Sen immediately turned his gaze from the graveyard, and sure enough, his ox had broken the rope and run away. He stood up abruptly, chasing after it as quickly as the wind, gesturing urgently to Ah Fu across the way:

"Ah Fu! Ah Fu! I'll cut over there! Stop it! Stop it!"

The ox, like a lion escaped from its cage, had regained its primitive nature of thousands of years ago, stamping its hooves violently, its tail cocked up angrily, its head lowered, its two horns flying like two arrows. It leaped over the mud clods like fish scales, it stepped on the withered yellow rice roots, it frightened away the flock of golden sparrows pecking at the desolate ears of grain, and leaped over the heads of the grass-cutting children, heading straight towards the graveyard.

Ah Sen gasped for breath, the tobacco pipe on his belt constantly hitting his hand, the long braid on his head constantly flicking his eyes, he was being hindered; while the beast seemed to be going faster and faster. He gasped, gasped, walked, walked, and finally saw the beast stop.

Standing on that desolate little hill, it was chewing on the tender green grass beside the graves, its tongue often reaching out to lick its steaming nostrils, its tail swaying leisurely. Surely, it thought this place was somewhere beyond the human world. Later, it wanted to regard the small hill as a wild mountain. Like other wild beasts in caves, it would make this its hometown. Later, it thought it would definitely be able to escape its fetters and labor entirely for itself in this paradise of its hometown. Surely, it also thought that later it would begin its beautiful life.

But this was still a place where Ah Sen could reach. He had already caught up, panting. He smiled and scolded:

"Beast! Beast! This is a graveyard! This is a graveyard!" He called out the word "graveyard" especially loudly, as if to say, "You're stepping into the grave!"

Seeing Ah Sen chasing after it, the beast returned to its primitive nature, digging its horns into the gaps in the graves. With a "whoosh," its head turned into the grave, but its tail was swaying leisurely and triumphantly outside the grave.

Ah Sen's laughter was even louder. This was almost the first mad laugh of his life. He rushed over, forcefully dragging its tail, trying to pull it out of the grave; all the while still laughing loudly.

The head in the grave angrily called out: "Moo!"

No one knew how, but suddenly it was as if a sharp arrow pierced Ah Sen's heart, and his laughter stopped abruptly. His rough fingers let go of the tail, hanging down like wooden chicken claws, and every wrinkle on his face was etched out. Whether it was sweat or tears, glistening with the color of the November sunlight, flowing down in a rustling stream from his staring eyes, from every wrinkle, from his dirty cloth shirt. He was stunned. He was thinking of the time when he had evaded rent and fled to a mountain cave, and later Old Boss Jin Rong had found him, dragging him out of the cave by his braid!

Glimpses of Ginza 193

— Wu Mu

In the blink of an eye, 1935 has reached "year's end." Japan's magazine industry is known for being ahead of schedule; next year's "New Year's" and "New Year's Issues" are already out. Newspapers these days are also filled with advertisements for major department stores' "Year-End Grand Raffle" and "Year-End Sale." If you go for a walk in the Ginza area at night, these days it's even more lively than in the past, everyone is busy, and women are even more busy going in and out of department stores buying things, buying gifts. It is the scene of preparing for the New Year.

Wherever you go, as soon as it's almost the New Year, it's always more lively than usual. But this "liveliness," sometimes although it looks lively on the surface, in reality it's often even more desolate than usual. Isn't Tokyo exactly like this?

Yes. Several of Tokyo's largest department stores, such as Mitsukoshi, Takashimaya, and Matsuzakaya, are all taking advantage of this "year-end" opportunity to hold "grand sales." Colorful goods are piled high in beautiful glass display windows, and the stores' "female clerks" are also more diligent in serving customers than usual, but buying things always requires money! Except for a small number of true "capitalists"; most middle-class or small property owners can only pick out a cheap item or two and that's it. Sometimes, after picking and choosing for a long time; they find the goods are really good; but in the end, the expression of having to give up because the price is too expensive can often be found on the faces of general shoppers. I don't know how many people run through the department stores in a day, but probably less than half of them actually buy something and leave?

For the "year-end" "grand raffle" and "grand sale"; the neon lights of Ginza are even more dazzling these days. Luxury, brilliance, and the sound of music drift everywhere. But right next to these largest dance halls or department stores, in the small alleys, there are people holding their own children, shivering and kneeling in the darkness begging for alms. When noble ladies and gentlemen pass by these beggars, their eyes disdain to even look at them; it's still "year-end," and these beggars have no way to participate in the "imperial ladies and gentlemen's" work of preparing for the New Year. I think, the existence of these beggars in the darkness is the greatest threat to Ginza's year-end prosperity. Because even if Ginza's department stores, bars, and dance halls' neon lights are brighter, the dark places are still more numerous than the bright places!

Wind and Cloud Part Two 194

— Fei Xiong

After the gloomy autumn, the winter wind and clouds blew in from the north.

A stone began to be taken from the heart, and flames suddenly sprouted in the winter rain and snow. Night. A long snake stretched out in the darkness, leaving darkness behind it. The clock struck, ringing out the cries long suppressed in the heart; cries awakened the resurrected dream.

Is the north wind blowing? Stirring up the waves of China. Is the dew heavy? Dripping away the troubled dreams from the heart.

With empty stomachs, staggeringly leaning on other people's shoulders; other people are leaning on other people's shoulders. Trudge on, the sky will brighten.

Shout, shout, even the shadows of the trees are swaying. What is tomorrow? What has tomorrow?

Tomorrow: Do your feet hurt? No, the road is long! Is your throat parched? There is nectar ahead.

Joy slipped from young people's mouths to young people's hearts; light flashed from young people's hearts to the hearts of the masses.

"There's bread to eat."

"Good!"

"We don't want bread!"

"Support ××!"

On the street:

The street is crowded with people, a wooden stick strikes down. Women pass by solemnly: belts stand solemnly. ×× people's armored cars are coming, blue-eyed fire trucks are coming.

The train glides along the tracks with a soft rumble.

Laugh! Laugh! Stand up straight!
