The Distance Between Leaving and Staying 195

— Xi Cun

If you have ever been unemployed, and for a very long period, when you are desperately seeking work and finally find a position, then you are the most aware of the true feelings involved. I mean, you can then imagine how diligent and devoted I would be to this newly acquired job. Truly, because I couldn't find work for so long, I almost despaired and fantasized about how best to commit suicide. People can do anything when they are at their wit's end.

From six in the evening to twelve midnight is the working time for my new job. In a typesetting room, nine of us dirty-handed workers are crammed together, covered head to toe in a layer of lead dust and grease. Although the meager pay is embarrassing to mention, I knew how to be punctual and work without laziness or shortcuts for this new job.

Logically, a typesetting workshop for night work should have particularly bright electric lights. But in reality, it wasn't so. Our dark room only had two electric lights, and the bulbs were only fifteen candlepower each. How could that possibly provide enough light? Fortunately, this unusually small room had no windows on three sides, and the only side with a window was blocked by a high wall, making it airtight. The darkness was actually a little brighter, but as a result, the stuffy air was more than enough for people to bear. Luckily, it was winter. If it were summer, I think the workers would certainly turn into sweat-soaked ghosts. Even the heat could kill several people a year.

Five of us were either typesetting or working as printers. The type cases were arranged in a dark, blurry array in the corner. The order in which they were arranged was based on the radical index of ordinary dictionaries. Before searching for a character, one had to first think about which radical it belonged to, which was both mentally and visually taxing. As a novice, I found it very inconvenient.

My colleague Zhao Mazi once offered the boss a suggestion on this matter, saying, "Boss, I think it would be best if these types were arranged according to the 'Four-Corner Code' character indexing method. It would definitely be much more convenient to find them in the future."

What is the "Four-Corner Code?" I didn't quite know. I guessed that this thing with a strange name must be difficult to learn. So, wasn't Zhao Mazi intentionally playing a joke on me, a newcomer? I didn't approve, who would pay attention to this strange way! But as luck would have it, before I could object, the boss refused first. He stroked his figure-eight mustache, took a puff of his water pipe, and said with a frown, "What four-corner, five-corner stuff, I don't understand those things. How did China get messed up? You know? It's all because of one trick here and another trick there! It's easier to deal with fewer tricks. The more there are, the easier it is to go wrong and the harder it is to get on the right track!"

"It's convenient, it's really fast to find characters," Zhao Mazi continued, disregarding the boss's bad mood, to supplement his opinion.

After hearing this, the boss put down his water pipe, glared at Zhao Mazi with a distorted face as if he wanted to swallow him whole, and said angrily, "No! No! A thousand times no! You say it's convenient, but I say it's inconvenient! Besides, can you guarantee that you'll work here for the rest of your life? If you leave here one day for a better job, what will happen to the people who come later who don't know the four-corner, five-corner stuff? Trying to be convenient will only add more trouble!"

I was so happy that I jumped up. The boss's words were exactly what I was thinking. I couldn't help but interject, "The boss is absolutely right. Zhao Mazi, put away your new tricks. Don't bother anymore and don't invite trouble for yourself."

What I will never forget is Zhao Mazi's angry glare at me at that moment, full of hostility. He shouted loudly, "You bastard, you want to chime in too? Why don't you go play cards to protect your eyes? Do you want to be blind!"

That night, after leaving the typesetting room, I felt uncomfortable as I walked along. Zhao Mazi shouldn't have called me a bastard in front of the boss. He was clearly insulting me! I wanted to find him and argue. Just then, he caught up with me from behind, panting heavily. As if he had seen through my intention to question and argue with him, he grabbed my shoulder, smiled, and said, "Brother, I beg you, don't be angry, okay? I have something to tell you."

I didn't answer, and I really got angry. I was blaming him. Seeing that I didn't say a word, it obviously caused him inner anxiety. He forcefully pulled my hand, held it tightly, and still smiled as he said to me:

"I was too reckless, but you are too suspicious. A worker doesn't speak according to books, you know. I was wrong, please forgive me this time."

"I'm not angry, so what do you want me to forgive you for?" I had originally planned to make a fuss, but now I felt a little embarrassed. I regretted that I was too narrow-minded. Zhao Mazi's uninhibited spirit was really admirable. My reply was very unnatural, and a clever person might think I was lying and still angry.

Zhao Mazi was straightforward enough. He completely believed my reply, and a sincere, friendly smile appeared on his face. He then changed the subject.

The streets were particularly quiet at midnight. This area was also secluded, so there were no vehicles coming and going. Besides the two of us, the only things moving were the cold winter wind and the shadows of the two of us, sometimes long and sometimes short, reflected under the streetlights.

"Brother, you are young," Zhao Mazi said after walking for a while, looking at me again, "Believe me, okay? You're not angry with me anymore, right? Let me tell you, do you know the ultimate benefit of being a typesetter? That benefit will get you two red eyes—all because you're searching for lead type and rolling around in it, ruining your eyes. I said using the 'Four-Corner Code' was for my own sake, to make searching easier and less strenuous on the eyes. You misunderstood my good intentions."

"But that's because I didn't know what the 'Four-Corner Code' was. I really thought it would add trouble, so I objected. To be honest, you didn't teach me how to use it, so you can't blame me."

Later, one day, after I learned the "Four-Corner Code" character indexing method from him, I really felt the convenience of the indexing itself and said to him, "Mazi, this method is good. I really misunderstood you before." I regretted that I had learned it so late and said apologetically, "Why didn't you tell me earlier? Wouldn't it have been good to cheer you on when you asked the boss to adopt it that time?" I really regretted that missed opportunity. I thought that if the two of us had suggested it together, the boss might have accepted our opinion. That would have been so good.

"It's not too late to talk about it now. As long as there's a reason, we can always talk about it."

Two days later, the two of us did indeed tell the boss about this idea. The two of us were the ones who took the lead, and the other partners also said some words of support from the side because they had all learned this new "Four-Corner Code" character indexing method.

"Hmph!" The boss first snorted, glanced at me, and asked back, "Xiao Liuzi, you're also saying these new tricks now? Didn't you disapprove of them before?"

"Because now I know that this method is really much more convenient."

"Much more convenient? I just don't want it to be convenient, see what you can do!" he said angrily, slamming the water pipe on the table. "Others say that the new bookkeeping method is convenient; I still use the old-fashioned ledger and haven't been killed by the inconvenience! Is it good to change things often? The ancestral methods are so precious, how can they be easily changed? Nonsense is simply bewitched! Fine, you go reform, go find a place with 'four-corner' and 'five-corner' methods to work at. I can't keep such talented people here! Consider it that I respect you!"

The business was therefore suspended. It was hard enough to find a job, and now I was unemployed again, which was really heartbreaking. At first, I still blamed Zhao Mazi's Four-Corner Code for harming people, but after thinking about it and understanding the business sense of the boss-type people, there was nothing to be unhappy about. Sooner or later, this small setback at work would happen anyway, so what did it matter!

Theft 196

Watching the Moon 197

— Zhou Muzhai

Not long after nightfall, I happened to raise my head from my desk. Then, leaning back in my chair, I saw the moon through the window across the courtyard, forming a diagonal line. It seemed like a discovery, and I couldn't help but say,

"There's a moon tonight!"

Immediately, I had another thought, "Today" is already the tenth day of the lunar month. There should have been one long ago. I was starting to feel a little regretful about saying those unconscious words, even though the words were also said unconsciously.

"Is this the first time you've seen the moon this month?" my wife asked, with a tone of surprise.

I was a little dazed: "The first time, what?"

"The first time you see the moon in a month, if you see it sitting down, you won't be busy this month. If you see it walking, you'll be busy. If you see it sleeping, you'll be even less busy."

"Is there such a saying?" But I knew what she meant.

"It's a common saying."

At first, I thought it was some kind of mental effect. Hearing "common saying," I thought, it's not accidental. Comparatively speaking, isn't walking busy? Isn't sitting idle? Isn't sleeping even more idle?

However, there is still a bit of leisure when walking and seeing the moon. "Appreciating the moon" and "walking by the moon" are different. Sitting doesn't necessarily mean seeing it, and sleeping is even more about falling asleep. Conversely, there are people who "watch the moon" while walking, sitting, and sleeping. This is considered "avoiding convention."

On Nibbling and Chewing Words 198

— Tang Tao

Since last year, there has been an issue that everyone has not paid much attention to, but which is actually quite important, namely the so-called "nibbling and chewing words." Although few people participated in the discussion, the opinions on this issue can still be divided into two factions. One faction is purely opposed to it, believing that nibbling and chewing words is not literature. To have good literature, one must learn from real life. The other faction, in addition to opposing the abuses of tradition, also gave nibbling and chewing words a new meaning, believing that appropriate nibbling and chewing of words is precisely the cultivation of literary skills.

My opinion is closer to the latter.

Mr. Xu Yanbo of the Tang Dynasty, when writing articles, always wrote Fengge as Yingge, Longmen as Qiuhu, Jingu as Xianxi, Yushan as Qiongyu, and Zhuma as Xiaocan. This was not to match the facts, but to seek depth and make it difficult to understand. This is chewing words. Mr. Kong Yiji, when he saw the children asking him for fennel beans, shook his head and said, "Not much, not much! Is it much? Not much." He was not writing a love poem, nor was he citing classics, but he insisted on finding phrases close to books. This is nibbling words. We should oppose such nibbling and chewing of words. People who use beautiful rhetoric and elegant language to disguise the emptiness of the content of their articles will only be rejected, opposed, and slowly decline in the literary world today.

But why do I also approve of nibbling and chewing words? Because the nibbling and chewing words I am talking about has a different new meaning. I believe that a person should be careful and prudent when writing or reading their own or other people's articles, and nibbling and chewing words fits this condition. What we want to nibble out and chew out is not beauty, superficiality, or elegance, but concise, clear, precise, correct, simple, and factual words.

Soviet new writers greatly admired the efforts of past classical writers to polish their works. Tolstoy rewrote "War and Peace" seven times, Lermontov had to revise a line several times, and Chekhov once said, "When a manuscript is finished, it must be allowed to lie down and heal." These things were spread among them and became beautiful stories. Why? Because the correct, concise, clear, and simple use of words must rely heavily on nibbling and chewing.

Recently, I read a passage in this journal:

"In the past, literati suffered greatly from the grinding of words, to the extent that some spent years on a single word and ten years on a single composition. Bai Letian's poems were all considered to have been revised by Yang Wenzhong Gong after he finished writing, pasted them on the wall, sat and lay down to observe them, corrected them to the best of his ability, and then showed them to others. Dazong once obtained several drafts of poems by Mr. Dongpo at Wangzhi's place, the grandson of Wenzhong Gong. His poem in response to Ou Shubi said: 'Yuanming as a small city, then circled it to write it down, changed it to find the word, and then smeared out the two words 'small city' to make 'county magistrate,' changing the word three times to form the current sentence. As for 'pepper in small amounts, why use eight hundred pecks,' he first said: 'pepper also why use,' then stored eight hundred pecks. If it were like the initial words, it would inevitably be criticized by future generations. It is also known that even great writers do not rely on momentary inspiration to determine the words, but are afraid of editing them."

Although we feel that spending years on a single word and ten years on a single composition is a bit too cautious and somewhat ridiculous. However, the fact remains that an important word must be carefully considered, and a great work should be nurtured for many years.

Shen Yiqing also has a statement:

"Ancient people did not abandon the method of refining words, but they won with meaning, not with words. One can see oddness in ordinary words, danger in common words, newness in old words, and color in plain words. Modern people who use words to show off their skills only make them difficult."

This also explains what we should nibble and chew. Yes, we need a rich vocabulary, but we do not advocate abandoning books. However, the books from which we absorb vocabulary must be modern and ordinary. On this point, because of the needs of reality, we can quote foreign, that is, so-called Europeanized, sentences, but we absolutely do not have to look for difficult words and ancient phrases in Zhuangzi and Wenxuan to "show off our skills."

This "unnecessary" is precisely the result of nibbling and chewing.

In addition to books, what is more important is to learn, adopt, and quote local languages from real life—especially local languages that everyone can understand. The important thing is selection. Doesn't selection prove that we still have to nibble and chew?

Great works must have accurate, rich, and moving content. But this accurate, rich, and moving content is conveyed by writers through words. Therefore, we also do not forget to seek the perfection of these words. In other words, we seek formal success.

In this way, we need to nibble and chew.

The procession moves forward,

Shanghai Da Sun Company Opening Special

Opening Declaration 200

Our company, Da Sun Co., Ltd., is affiliated with Hong Kong Da Sun Co., Ltd. It was founded in the first year of the Republic of China. Branches and stores were subsequently established on Xidi and Huiai Middle Road in Guangzhou, operating department stores and also engaging in hotel, restaurant, and rooftop garden businesses. Adhering to the principle of sincerity and mutual trust, we have striven to operate diligently without any slackening. We have been deeply favored by people from all walks of life. Over the past two decades, our business has made considerable progress. While feeling encouraged, we have been thinking about how to better serve the community. Therefore, we raised funds to organize a Shanghai branch some time ago. Now, fortunately, the new building has been completed and business has begun. We are willing to continue to serve the society with the same principles of sincerity and trustworthiness. We will do our utmost to promote domestic products, working together with manufacturers to facilitate sales. As we are just beginning our business, our facilities may not be complete. We sincerely hope that people from all walks of life will come and patronize us and provide guidance. We would be extremely grateful. This declaration is made for your consideration.

Respectfully,

Cai Chang, General Supervisor of Shanghai Da Sun Co., Ltd.

The Position of Da Sun Department Store 201

— Julean Arnold, U.S. Commercial Attaché to China

Citizens benefit greatly from a well-organized department store. Because of its thorough planning and huge investment, it can collect goods from all sources and therefore offer surprisingly low prices. This is something that small-scale merchants cannot hope to match. A department store gathers all kinds of goods under one roof. Showcases stand in rows, and everything is in good order. Customers can see everything at a glance and can get what they want without having to wander through the streets. Moreover, the prices are fixed, so there is no need to haggle. The staff is sincere and provides excellent service. In addition, the organization is Chinese-owned and has extensive experience. It is only natural that its threshold is worn through and its business is booming.

With skilled workers and excellent materials, a magnificent building has been built. The painted beams and carved rafters of the grand pavilion reach into the clouds. The towering building is high and commanding. Its novel facilities include escalators, so customers can move from floor to floor without lifting a foot. The displays in its windows and corridors are magnificent, and the ladies who visit are all delighted.

Chinese department stores are more advanced than their American counterparts in terms of entertainment facilities. They have everything from singing and dancing to banquets, tea gardens, and cinemas, taking into account both trade and art. This is truly a unique feature.

Department stores collect goods from all over the world. Treasures from all corners of the earth are displayed in one room, earning it the nickname "permanent international exposition." They also display countless Chinese handicrafts, which are beautiful beyond compare. Ladies from Europe and America who are traveling and stop in Shanghai can visit the store to observe the actual development of Chinese industry. Therefore, department stores are eager to promote inexpensive and exquisite indigenous products. In addition to presenting foreign products, department stores play a very important role in the country's industry.

A General Description of Shanghai Da Sun Company 202

— Jianwen

Shanghai is a port city with a dense population and a mix of Chinese and foreigners. It is the focus of attention both at home and abroad and is the only major port in the East. The promotion of domestic products is a major priority here, and the city is closely related to the world economy and domestic finance. Moreover, construction has been progressing rapidly in recent years. The Greater Shanghai Plan is being realized, and magnificent buildings are everywhere. Now, between Nanjing Road, Xizang Road, and Labour Road, there is another towering structure that rises into the clouds. The location is convenient for transportation, with a constant flow of traffic. It is a sight that attracts everyone's attention. What is it? It is the Da Sun Company, which is officially opening today.

Da Sun Company, as the name suggests, is undoubtedly grand in scale and novel in its facilities. However, Da Sun Company is not only refreshing in Shanghai, but also a leader among department stores in China. The company was founded in Hong Kong in the first year of the Republic of China. It has also operated two branches in Guangzhou for more than 20 years. It has always been committed to serving the community, with fixed prices and small profits and large sales. Therefore, people from all walks of life have praised it and regarded it as the only place to buy goods. The success of the Hong Kong and Guangzhou branches is not accidental.

Now, in view of the need for a new type of department store in Shanghai, the company has actively prepared for and added a Shanghai branch. It has now been completed and will continue to operate with its original purpose, striving to meet the expectations of the community. Its facilities and features are briefly described below:

(1) Beautiful Architecture: The company's building stands between Nanjing Road, Xizang Road, and Labour Road, occupying eight acres of land. It is ten stories high and built using the steel-frame concrete construction method. It was designed by the local Jitai Engineering Firm. The latest architectural principles were adopted for the light and air throughout the building. The exterior walls are made of domestic milky-yellow glazed ceramic tiles, and the facade is made of black granite from Qingdao. The interior floors are paved with Italian stone, and the second and third floors are covered with rubber and teak floors. The interior and exterior are extremely clean and beautiful.

(2) New-Style Elevators: The company's new-style elevators are fast and comfortable. The opening and closing of the elevator doors are automatic and do not require human labor. Customers find them very convenient to use.

(3) Lighting: Department stores are public places where all kinds of goods are displayed and crowds gather, so it is necessary to ensure that the lighting is suitable. Moreover, in order to accurately identify the color of the goods being selected, accurate lighting is essential. Therefore, the company has paid special attention to the lighting, so that customers who enter the building feel refreshed and are very satisfied with their selection of goods. This is enough to show the novelty of the company's facilities and its consideration for customers.

(4) Climate: Adjusting the indoor temperature is a major issue in modern new building facilities. The company has paid close attention to this point. The interior is equipped with heating and cooling pipes, so there is no severe cold in winter and no extreme heat in summer, creating an image of perpetual spring.

(5) Escalators: Department stores are distributed over several floors, and customers who are shopping are inevitably inconvenienced by having to go up and down. Therefore, recent great buildings have been equipped with elevators for going up and down. However, they are still insufficient when customers are crowded. In view of this, the company has not only installed the latest type of elevators, but has also added two escalators, which run directly from the pavement to the third floor. This is the first installation of its kind in the country. Customers only need to stand on it to go up and down the stairs steadily and quickly. This is a unique innovation in vertical transportation facilities.

(6) Goods Display: The arrangement of the various goods in a department store requires a lot of study. The connectivity of the categories, the cleanliness of the layout, and the convenience of supply are all related to the psychology and selection of customers. The company has paid special attention to this and has ensured that the pedestrian areas are spacious to avoid crowding and create a comfortable atmosphere.

(7) Department Configuration: The company is currently using the first to fourth floors as commercial areas, and the fifth floor and above as entertainment venues. It is located in the bustling center of Shanghai, and the grand racecourse is in front of it. The square offers a clear view and fresh air, which is not easy to find in other bustling areas. The internal distribution is listed below as a guide.

Basement: Southern goods, ham, sea cucumber and bird's nest, hardware, and inexpensive goods.

Ground Floor: Canned food, biscuits, fruit, foreign wines, cigars and cigarettes, camera materials, thermos bottles, eyeglasses, stationery, Chinese and Western medicines, cosmetics and fragrances, Western clothing, straw hats and felt hats, cotton underwear, head brushes and combs, handkerchiefs and towels, silk and wool socks, women's handbags, umbrellas, wallets, gift certificates, and flowers.

Second Floor: Felt carpets, silverware, ivory enamelware, watches from all over the world, telescopes, musical instruments, toys, furniture, leather trunks, Fuzhou lacquerware, Jiangxi porcelain, glass porcelain, and electrical appliances.

Third Floor: Gauze silks and satins, wool and cloth, fine wool fabrics, Chinese and Western clothing, Beijing-Suzhou clothing trim, women's clothing, children's clothing, and Chinese and Western boots and shoes.

Fourth Floor: General office, purchasing department, warehouse, and product exhibition hall.

Ten-Story Building Built by Shanghai Da Sun Co., Ltd. 203

Page 18

Summary of the Architectural Plan of the Shanghai Da Sun Company 204

— Architect: Kee Tai Engineering Firm

Location

The location is at the western end of Nanjing Road, Shanghai, bordering streets on three sides, occupying 200 feet of Nanjing Road, and 320 feet each of Lloyd Road and Tibet Road, totaling an area of 8.2 mu. The location is ideal, adjacent to major department stores, major hotels, and amusement parks.

Size

The storefront on Nanjing Road is 190 feet east-west and 220 feet north-south, covering an area of 430 square zhang, or 5.5 mu. The four floors above ground and the basement are used for commercial space, while the upper four floors and the rooftop are used for amusement facilities and a rooftop garden. The total height from the ground to the roof is 127 feet, with a total of ten floors including the basement. The highest point accessible to visitors is 140 feet. The total volume of the building is estimated to be 5 million cubic feet, making it one of the largest buildings in Shanghai.

Basement

The basement is designed as a commercial space, a common practice in many countries, but a pioneering effort in Shanghai. The Da Sun Company management carefully considered this plan and believed that it would be highly beneficial to both the company and its customers. However, thorough planning was required for damp-proofing and transportation. Currently, the southern side of the basement is a sales area, occupying two-thirds of the total area. In addition to elevators, there are four grand staircases in the front and rear connecting to the upper-level storefront entrances, and one staircase in the middle connecting to the middle floor for convenience. Receiving and delivery facilities are also attached to benefit customers. The northwest corner is the machine room, which is not connected to the storefront and can be accessed directly from the outer courtyard. The northeast corner is the area for receiving goods, unpacking, and temporary storage, with a separate exit.

The basement is nine feet below ground, with a four-foot space under the floor to provide damp-proofing and space for various pipes. All exterior walls are made of reinforced concrete with damp-proofing measures.

Mr. Cai Chang, General Supervisor of Da Sun Company 205

First Floor

With entrances on three sides facing the street, there are a total of seven entrances, four staircases leading to the upper-level shopping area, three passenger elevators, one freight elevator, and one pneumatic tube delivery system. The locations of these staircases have been carefully studied to ensure proper distribution and convenient transportation. In addition, there is an escalator from the first floor to the second floor, which is unique among Shanghai companies. Located in the middle, each elevator can transport 4,000 people per hour, eliminating concerns about waiting and crowding. Customers can stand and ascend, with an unobstructed view of the store's interior, which is even more convenient.

The first floor has a total of 3,000 feet of counters, the most among major companies in Shanghai. The walkways are as wide as eleven feet, preventing overcrowding.

The three sides of the first floor facing the street have a mezzanine, used for staff rest and storage. The central atrium is 130 feet square and 19 feet high, providing ample space and ventilation.

The interior decoration of the department store and shops is mainly simple and harmonious, as customers' attention is on the goods, not the building. Therefore, except for the Italian marble floor and the plain ceiling using new construction methods, all small beams are eliminated except for the main beams.

Second, Third, and Fourth Floors

All are shopping areas, with each floor having 3,400 square feet of space, four staircases, and three elevators directly accessible from the lower floors. Each floor has restrooms for men and women. The internal counter arrangements have been carefully studied before installation.

The southern part of the fourth floor is the Da Sun Company's office, the western part is the warehouse, the eastern part is a tea room, and the central part is a product display area, providing guidance for customers' shopping and promotion for domestic manufacturers. This is another special contribution of Da Sun Company to Shanghai society.

Fifth Floor to the Top

All four floors are public entertainment areas, namely amusement parks. According to the current plan, the fifth floor is reserved for a large theater, the sixth floor is a cinema, and the rest are divided into various amusement activities. Separate staircases and four elevators are provided on Lloyd Road and Tibet Road for access to these floors, not connected to the commercial area.

It is estimated that the entertainment area of the entire building can accommodate 20,000 spectators at the same time. When the facilities are completed and the opening ceremony is held, it can be considered the largest popular amusement park in Shanghai.

Magnificent Appearance

Department store buildings are naturally judged by their size, so this building strives for simplicity, with a slight Chinese style, and the rich colors are all on the upper floors to match the amusement park area. The lower part of the large awning is the display window area, using more luxurious materials, namely Chinese black labradorite, while the upper floors use tiles, striving for simplicity and lasting beauty.

Construction Method

Undertaken in stages, the piling work is carried out first, with a total of 214 piles of 110 feet long and 862 piles of 90 feet long. The civil engineering work, from the foundation to the roof, is all constructed with reinforced concrete frames, striving for solidity. The internal and external walls are all made of hollow bricks. All other materials, such as floor slabs, are fireproof materials, so the entire building is fireproof, durable, and the entire reinforced concrete plan has been carefully studied to save costs, with all beams and columns kept simple.

Other Facilities

In addition to civil engineering, there are still electrical wiring, heating, sanitation, and fire protection components. The first floor and basement are equipped with the latest air-conditioning pipes to purify the air and facilitate the preservation of goods. The entire building is equipped with heating and cooling fans (Unit Heater), and the temperature inside the shopping area is more than ten degrees higher than outside, providing comfort for customers. Each floor is equipped with toilets and sanitary facilities, and the entire building is equipped with fire sprinkler systems, further ensuring the safety of goods and customers.

A Visit to the Da Sun Company 206

— (Zhen Yi)

On the morning of January 3rd, in the piercing north wind, Mr. Yao Junwei and I went to visit Mr. Liang Bingjian at the temporary office of the Da Sun Company on Tibet Road. Although the office was located in a few ordinary houses, the intense and active work of the internal staff, full of a vigorous spirit of enterprise, gave outsiders a fresh feeling upon entering the door. Mr. Liang is the company's chief accountant. Although he is also from Guangdong, he has lived in Shanghai for many years, so he speaks fluent Shanghainese. He humbly invited us to rest for a while and then led us to visit the new building. We started from the bottom floor. The basement construction is deeply buried underground and includes the southern goods section, ginseng and bird's nest section, hardware and blood tonic section, bargain section, and furnace room, among other sections. The perimeter of the building is equipped with hot and cold air ducts. It is said that whether it is the scorching summer or the severe winter, the temperature inside can always be maintained between sixty and seventy degrees, warm as spring all year round, making people feel very comfortable. The glass counters in each section have also been meticulously designed. The joints at each corner do not use wooden columns but are inlaid with a delicate metal, allowing customers walking past the counters to have a clear view of the goods displayed inside, without obstructing anyone's line of sight. Next to the furnace room is a cloakroom for employees to hang their clothes. The Da Sun Company has a total of more than 600 employees, and more than 100 of them have received practical training at the head office and branches in Hong Kong and Guangzhou. When they serve in the future, they will all wear neat uniforms, and each person will hang their clothes according to their own number. Moreover, there are two large doors for entry and exit, so that good order can be maintained without confusion and crowding. The basement is very spacious, with light

Canned Goods Section of the Storefront 207

Page 19

and air being properly considered. Therefore, being there will never make you imagine that this is a basement.

The first floor of the store sells gift certificates, flowers, canned food, candies and biscuits, fruits, foreign wine, cigars, cigarettes, camera supplies, hot and cold water bottles, stationery, Chinese and Western medicines, cosmetics, Western-style clothing, straw hats, felt hats, cotton underwear, head combs, handkerchiefs, towels, silk and wool socks, women's handbags, umbrellas, wallets, and other items. The first floor of the store has a total of six large doors, and another door is specifically for accessing the amusement park. Therefore, even if there are crowds, there will never be a problem with particularly crowded entrances. The automatic elevators from the first floor of the basement have a total of six, and the drivers are female employees. The opening and closing of the elevator doors are automated by machines, without the need for manual labor from the drivers. This is also a rare new facility in Shanghai. In addition, there is also a motorized escalator, in the same form as ordinary stairs. Passengers only need to stand on the steps to ascend or descend quickly, without feeling dizzy and with convenience and speed. Each step can only accommodate one person, and it can carry more than 4,000 passengers per hour. At this time, the foreign engineer who built the escalator happened to be nearby. According to him, the application of this escalator is already widespread in foreign department stores or large institutions, but in China, the Da Sun Company is the first to install and use it. As he spoke, he led us to try it out, going all the way through the second floor and reaching the third floor, which indeed made people feel convenient and novel. It is expected that on the day of the opening, many people will be curious to try it out.

The second floor has billiards, bedding, silverware, enamelware, ivory, clocks and watches from various countries, telescopes, eyeglasses, musical instruments, toys, furniture, leather suitcases, trunks, Fuzhou lacquerware, glass and porcelain, electrical materials, electric lights, and other sections. When we visited, the porcelain section had already been arranged. These porcelains were designed with new styles by the company and then custom-made in Jiangxi, so not only is the quality excellent, but the style and patterns are also very modern. The second floor has gauze, silk, woolen cloth, fine furs, Chinese and Western clothing, Beijing-Suzhou clothing trims, women's clothing, children's clothing, Chinese and Western boots and shoes, and other sections. The equipment such as counters and clothes racks paid close attention to avoiding obstructing customers' view.

The shopping area includes four floors including the basement. After careful observation of the various facilities on each floor, I know that they really put a lot of effort into the design during construction. The fourth floor is the main office, with several rooms built in a separated manner. This can avoid the noise of guests talking and disrupting the mood of the staff. In front of the main office, there is a very wide area, which will be used for exhibiting goods or other works of art in the future. The fourth floor is prepared to set up a cafeteria, selling food and wine as economically as possible, so that the general salaried class working near Nanjing Road can spend very little money to eat a delicious meal here. From the fifth floor onwards, it is all amusement park areas. When we went up to visit, the workers were diligently doing decoration work, and everything was not yet ready. When it is arranged in the future, it will be a popular entertainment area with a variety of performances and melodious songs. We went all the way to the roof, where the howling north wind cracked people's skin, making people tremble. Looking down, the scenery of the whole of Shanghai is clearly visible, and the pedestrians and vehicles are as small as lice and squirming in the dust. This is truly a spectacle.

It took a total of two hours to see a rough overview of the new building of Da Sun Company. Finally, I thanked Mr. Liang, who led us on the visit, and went back with a satisfied mood.

What I Hope for from the Da Sun Company 209

— (Zhen Yi)

The Da Sun Company, which has appeared in Shanghai with a new attitude with modern business methods and modernized architecture, has opened today! It will shake the Shanghai market and be active on the commercial battlefield. In today's sluggish economy, we have endless hopes for the opening of the Da Sun Company. We deeply hope that the colleagues of this large company can practice the following points.

(1) Strive to promote domestic products. Our country has suffered from the economic invasion of the great powers for several decades! Now our national economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the social crisis is deepening day by day. If we do not rise up to promote domestic products and recover our rights, then the disaster of national subjugation will be imminent. At this stage of national crisis, in today's surging social depression, we feel that we cannot bear to ask whether any department stores specializing in foreign goods will be produced again; but on the other hand, we urgently need a large-scale modern department store to promote domestic products. In the past, the Da Sun Company has had a good reputation among the social elites for serving the society and promoting domestic products in Hong Kong and Guangzhou. Now we hope that they will be more active in promoting domestic products in Shanghai. Although the great task of promoting domestic products is by no means something that a department store selling goods can simply take on, we always sincerely hope that they will try their best to unite with domestic manufacturers and cooperate to do this work. We know very well that in recent years, the production of domestic goods has made great leaps forward. There are many products that can simply overwhelm imported goods, but because the promoters are not good at their methods, even if there are good domestic goods, customers find it difficult to identify them, or simply do not know about them. With the great scale of the Da Sun Company and decades of commercial experience, if they can strive to promote domestic products, then I think the future of the domestic goods industry will definitely be greatly benefited, in other words, it can benefit both the society and the country.

(2) Uphold the credit of fixed prices. The Da Sun Company has always used fixed prices, honesty, and no deception as the basic principles of its business. We have seen that their business practices in Hong Kong and Guangzhou are like this, and now the opening declaration of the Shanghai Da Sun Company also clearly writes the words of adhering to the true meaning of fixed prices, which makes us very gratified! At the same time, we hope that they will always maintain this good principle and not be shaken by accommodating the environment. Because the original purpose of trading is to exchange what you have for what you don't have, each getting what they want, and neither party can cheat. Merchants in ancient times attached great importance to credit and honesty, and we should maintain this good habit. Although the Shanghai commercial environment has now been spoiled by some shops that are blinded by profit, making both buyers and sellers meticulous and haggling over prices, it is not impossible for the Da Sun Company to reverse this decline if it can adhere to the credit of fixed prices. The environment can be transformed by human effort, which is a belief that every business operator should have.

(3) Pay attention to service ethics. It is an undeniable fact that Chinese stores do not pay attention to service ethics. We hope that the colleagues working at the Da Sun Company can pay special attention to service ethics in the future, so that general customers, no matter how much goods they buy or how much business they do, feel satisfied and leave a good impression. At the same time, it can also let foreigners in Shanghai know that our Chinese modern stores have also paid attention to service ethics, changing their traditional bad impression of Chinese merchants.

(4) Focus on the needs of the masses. Since stores serve the society, the target of service should be the general public in the society. Therefore, whether in terms of sales or equipment, it should be based on adapting to the needs of the masses, and not just thinking about a few people, because the Da Sun Company must make the general public have a good impression in their minds that "the Da Sun Company is the ideal supplier of our daily necessities," and should not make it become a market only for a few people in the society. At the same time, in these years of poverty and exhaustion, the purchase of goods should be based on practicality and economy, and the selling price should also be reduced as much as possible, implementing a policy of low prices and high sales.

The backbone of the entire building (that is, steel and wood) are all foreign materials, and cement and bricks are domestic products. The entire project was completed very quickly. The preliminary project for each floor was completed in only eight days, and the construction cost a total of 1.5 million yuan. The entire construction of 'Da Sun' was built by adopting the typical style of large-scale department stores in Europe and the United States. The installation of things such as rolling doors, escalators, automatic elevators, and various counters has been carefully designed and built. When we enter other department stores, we only see twists and turns, and people's heads are moving, sometimes making it impossible for people to find what they want to buy; but in the new building of 'Da Sun', customers can see everything at a glance as soon as they enter each floor, and it is easy to find the categorized goods. At the same time, because the internal facilities are perfect, the light is sufficient and bright, and the air is well-regulated, it gives people a good impression, and it is generally recognized as the 'ideal department store.'" Because Mr. Jin was very busy with official duties, he stopped there and hurriedly shook hands with the reporter.

Flourishing Business of China Stone Company 213

Among the large buildings in Shanghai that have recently been completed are the 22-story building of the Four Lines Savings Society on Jing'an Temple Road and the 9-story building of the Da Sun Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road. Both of these buildings are extremely majestic and magnificent. The internal and external stone materials, except for a small part of Italian marble, are all made of granite and Jade Buddha stone from the China Stone Company of Qingdao. What is most worthy of showing off in Shanghai is the outer wall of the ground floor, which is made of black labradorite, a special product of the Stone Company. This kind of stone material is only produced in Egypt besides my country's Shandong and Guizhou provinces. It also produces this kind of black labradorite. Its composition is mainly alkaline feldspar, amphibole feldspar, and hypersthene, which is obviously good and has no mica stone, so it is not afraid of the acidic effect of the hot sun and ice and frost. It is most suitable for use as an outer wall covering. Once polished, it is as bright as a mirror without the need to constantly wax it like foreign cloud stone, and it will not be peeled off by wind and frost after a long time. Therefore, recently, the special product of China Stone Company, black labradorite, has been sold to the Yangtze River area, such as the Bank of Communications in Nanjing, the Capital Hotel, the Dahua Grand Theater, the China Industrial Bank in Hankou, and the Meifeng Bank and Sichuan-Jian Bank in Chongqing, Sichuan. Overseas, places such as Java in Nanyang have successively ordered goods. At this time in our country, when legal currency is implemented and freight is inflated, among building materials, except for steel and hardware, there are no equivalent domestic products that can be used as substitutes. As for stone materials, due to the vastness of our country's land and the richness of its reserves, the China Stone Company collects a wide range of precious stones from famous mountains in various provinces, and processes and polishes them according to scientific methods. It must not allow Italian marble to monopolize the beauty of the past. It is hoped that the domestic construction industry will recover its rights in time and strive to promote it. Then the future of the Stone Company is still promising, and encourage it.

One of the New Facilities of the Da Sun Company 214

— Dong

Otis Escalators and Elevators: Convenience for Customers, Novel Styles

The architecture of the Da Sun Company is magnificent. There are countless new facilities. Otis escalators are one of them. The reason why the company installed Otis escalators is that the company's department store has a variety of goods, and the location is very wide. Without this latest type of escalator, it is really not enough to meet the needs of customers. Moreover, after installing this escalator, the goods can also be sold quickly. The sales volume is large, and the selling price can also be indirectly reduced, so it can also benefit customers.

The company has a total of two Otis escalators. One is from the basement to the second floor, and the other is from the second floor to the third floor. The appearance is very beautiful. Both of these can go up or down at the same time. The speed of each chain is nearly 90 feet per minute. Therefore, it can provide 4,000 people to move up and down per hour. In terms of twelve hours a day, it can be used by 48,000 customers. When the company's business hours are about to end at night, the two escalators can go down at the same time. Customers do not have to wait. They can go down smoothly and do not have to take steps. The convenience and comfort can be imagined.

When customers purchase goods from the company, everything is convenient. Even the goods located on the second and third floors can be purchased as conveniently as on the first floor.

Not only that, the company is also equipped with the latest self-leveling Otis elevators, a total of six. Five are for passengers, and one is for transporting goods. This type of elevator is completely self-leveling. The reason is that ordinary elevators often do not level with the ground when they stop, and management is not easy. Drivers often have the disadvantage of slow operation. Now using Otis self-leveling elevators, customers can enter and exit conveniently. The management is also very flexible. Just press the button and you will immediately reach the designated location. At present, the lower floors are open first. In the future, all actions will be carried out, and there will be a single special express train that can directly go to the upper-level amusement park. The elevator is located at the entrance of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road. The interior is very spacious and can accommodate twenty-four people. The speed is four hundred feet per minute. There are two more elevators, installed at the rear of the company on Tibet Road and Lloyd Road, which can directly reach the roof garden.

The decoration and equipment of the five elevators are all of the latest styles. There are two elevators in the company's store that can automatically open the doors and use electricity, which is very convenient.

The elevator action signs outside the elevator doors on each floor are also very clear, which is very different from ordinary elevators. This type of elevator equipment is only available in the Shanghai Electric Power Company (two), the Continental Building (two), the International Hotel (three), and the Broadway Apartments (several). Other companies do not have this type of elevator. It can be seen that the company's equipment is exquisite and that Otis elevators are of excellent quality.

A General Overview of the Sincere Company 215

— Huang

Its architecture, decor, equipment, and management are all exquisitely crafted. It is Shanghai's only modern and outstanding department store, striving to promote the sale of designed and improved goods for a way out.

The Sincere Company's new building, constructed over a year at a cost of over a million yuan, now stands majestically on the corner of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road. I, the writer, visited yesterday and was guided through the entire building by Mr. Liang of the company. I will now describe its general situation as follows.

History of Sincere: The Sincere Company was established by overseas Chinese from Australia, Mr. Cai Xing and Mr. Cai Chang, among others. In 1912, they gathered comrades and raised four million yuan to establish the Sincere Department Store in Hong Kong. Subsequently, in 1916, they established a branch in Guangzhou. Over the years, business has flourished and reputation has grown. Recognizing the importance of Shanghai's commercial position, they decided, after careful consideration, to build a large building and establish a company in Shanghai. Now, the new building has been completed and officially opened today. With the company's strong financial resources, outstanding reputation, and the founders' rich commercial experience and talent, it goes without saying that the Sincere Company's business will flourish day by day, with unlimited prospects. The new company has a capital of six million yuan. Mr. Hui Min, the manager of Sincere Hong Kong, has been transferred to serve as the manager. Mr. Cai Chang is the general supervisor.

Overview of the New Building: The Sincere Company's new building was constructed starting on November 19, 1934. It was designed by the Kee Yuen Engineering Firm and built by the Fook Kee Construction Company. From the start of construction to completion, it took thirteen months, with construction costs reaching over a million yuan. The new building has ten floors, from the basement to the roof, soaring into the sky and magnificent beyond compare. The entire building is based entirely on modern architectural principles, using the latest methods and specialized techniques, and constructed with the best materials. It is beautifully decorated and imposing. It has exhausted the possibilities of architectural aesthetics and artistry. Such a magnificent and grand department store building is not only unique in the country but also rare in Western countries. The new building is located at the corner of Nanjing Road, Tibet Road, and Lloyd Road, a prosperous location with wide streets. Customer parking is convenient. The richness of its interior decoration, the grandeur of its location, the ventilation, the brightness of the light, and other aspects are all outstanding and attractive. The ground floor has seven entrances, one of which leads directly to the rooftop amusement park, making it extremely convenient for both shoppers and general visitors to enter and exit.

Internal Layout: Five floors of the new building are used for the commercial area. The basement is used for storage, boiler rooms, the southern goods department, and the discount department, displaying various daily necessities throughout the year. The ground floor and the second and third floors display a wide range of goods, categorized and arranged in order. Departments such as fabrics and silks are located on the third floor, while departments such as clocks, toys, and furniture are located on the second floor. On the fourth floor, in addition to a portion of the area being used as an exhibition hall, the rest is used for accounting rooms, receiving rooms, and the general office. The fifth floor and above, up to the roof, are used as an amusement park. Currently, they are busy constructing stages and seats, hoping to complete them soon in order to attract various high-class entertainment performances to entertain visitors.

Various Facilities: The Sincere Company has all the latest facilities to enhance customer convenience and comfort. Among the most noteworthy are the hot and cold air ducts, the escalators that have never been seen in our country, and the uniquely designed special display cases. The hot and cold air ducts regulate the climate, making it warm as spring in winter and cool and breezy in summer, naturally making people feel happy. The escalators that quickly connect the ground floor and the second and third floors allow customers to ascend and descend easily by simply stepping onto the moving escalator steps, in addition to taking the three self-leveling elevators or the regular stairs. The escalators do not move too quickly, so while ascending and descending, one can look around and survey the entire area in order to select their favorite items. Each step is just large enough for one person to stand on, moving in sequence, making it a pleasant and comfortable experience without crowding. This is the special feature of the escalators. As for being absolutely safe and without danger, that goes without saying. The glass display cases for displaying goods, their installation method, and the corner seams are all designed and custom-made by the Sincere Company itself. They are very easy to install and remove and do not obstruct the view. All the goods in the display cases, whether they are in the corners of the cases or in the center, are clearly visible to customers from the outside.

Attentive Service: In order to ensure that customers receive maximum satisfaction and extreme comfort, the Sincere Company strives for perfection in terms of facilities and also pays great attention to service. All employees are trained to treat each customer with humility, enthusiasm, and sincerity, regardless of the size of the transaction.

Efforts to Promote Domestic Products: The Sincere Company's greatest goal is to promote domestic products and improve domestic production. Therefore, it not only adopts and promotes domestic products as much as possible, but also works with domestic manufacturers to research and improve them so that they can be sold effectively in the most modern and outstanding market, leading to increased production. With increased production and sales, industry and commerce will naturally flourish. This is of great benefit to society and the country. The Sincere Company is committed to this goal and is making every effort to achieve it. The various goods displayed in its various departments, such as silks, porcelain, and woodenware, are all domestic products. The beautiful and elegant new styles that make people reluctant to let go are all designed and custom-made by the Sincere Company. This shows its enthusiasm for promoting domestic goods. In terms of domestic goods, the Sincere Company's efforts go beyond this. In addition to collecting all kinds of domestic products, Sincere also procures the latest and best products from all over the world. This not only supplements the insufficient supply of domestic products but also serves as a model for imitation in order to manufacture high-quality domestic goods that are truly suitable for current needs.

The Chinese and Western Shoe Department on the Third Floor 216

Recent Situation of the Wah Hsin Brick & Tile Company 217

The Wah Hsin Brick & Tile Company has been established for over ten years. Its products, mainly large and small green and red flat tiles, have been sold in Shanghai and nearby ports and praised by the construction industry. Since Mr. Liu Zixian took over, the products have been greatly improved. In the past five or six years, the types have increased, including Spanish-style barrel tiles and Chinese temple-style barrel tiles, all of which are available. Two years ago, Mr. Liu saw that there was a great need for cement floor tiles (commonly known as patterned tiles) on the market, but most of the products were of poor quality and difficult to maintain. Those who tried them once regarded them as inferior products and rarely bought them again. He spent several months researching and realized that it was difficult to meet the market demand without improving the manufacturing process. Therefore, he purchased the latest machinery and adopted the latest methods to manufacture various colored cement floor tiles. Once they were launched, they spread like wildfire. In the past two years, many large and small buildings in the city and elsewhere have purchased them. Recently, the official residence of the President of the National Government in Nanjing, the Grand Hall of the National Government, the Party History Museum of the Central Party Headquarters, the Capital Hotel, the Jiangsu Bank, the Zhejiang Agricultural College in Hangzhou, the gymnasium of the Central Aviation School, the affiliated middle school of Soochow University in Huzhou, the office building of the Jiangxi Provincial Government in Nanchang, the Central Aviation Branch School, the Jiujiang Central Bank, the Haizhou Lianyungang Station Electric Factory, the Lagrene Children's Public School of the Shanghai French Municipal Council, the residence of Mr. Du Yuesheng, the residence of senior staff of the Bank of China, and the Sincere Company, which opened today, have all used Wah Hsin patterned floor tiles. There are countless other city houses and residences that have used them, which shows the excellent quality of the company's products.

Wah Hsin floor tiles are solid in texture, requiring a pressure of about 4,500 pounds per square inch. The colors are pure mineral and contain no impurities. The manufacturing method is novel, so the patterns are very clear, like paintings. The tile surface is smooth, not much less than glass. With these four advantages, it is appropriate that the construction industry regards it as a major innovation in cement floor tiles in the brick and tile industry today.

Mr. Liu Zixian, the manager and engineer of the company, studied in the United States and served as the chief engineer of the Taishan Brick & Tile Company and the manager and engineer of the Southeast Brick & Tile Company. He has excellent knowledge and rich experience and is a brick and tile expert. It is no accident that the company's products are excellent.

The Porcelain Department on the Second Floor 218

Characteristics of Domestic Magnetic Face Tiles 219

The magnetic face tiles used in the entire new Sincere Company building are produced by the New Machine Tile Factory on Zhoujiazui Road. These tiles are made entirely of Chinese clay. After applying oil to the tile surface, they are fired in one go, making them extremely strong, beautiful, and durable. They do not collect dust and are not easily damaged by wind, frost, rain, or snow. They are the most successful domestic product. Sincere Company decided to adopt them in large quantities first, which will greatly help the future development of purely domestic products.

Advantages of Datong Steel Windows 220

Modern buildings mostly use steel doors and windows for their beautiful style, flexible opening and closing, no hiding of insects and ants, durability, ample light, and fire prevention. However, if the products are not from a manufacturer with established experience and outstanding achievements, they often have the disadvantages of not being tightly sealed, leaking wind and rain, and being frequently damaged. All the steel windows of the Sincere Company were contracted to the famous Datong Steel Window Company in Shanghai. They are beautiful and strong, different from other companies. This proves the Datong Steel Window Company's experience and achievements in the steel window business.

The Southern Goods Department in the Basement 221
